<pr_description>
# Bug Report: Config Import Fails with "metaDataItem is null" Error
# Bug Report: Config Import Fails with "metaDataItem is null" Error

## Description

The configuration import feature in Nacos 3.x console does not work properly. When attempting to import configurations via ZIP file, the server returns an error indicating that `metaDataItem` is null. Additionally, the exported ZIP files from the console also lack the necessary `meta_data` file, making it impossible to re-import exported configurations.

## Steps to Reproduce

### Case 1: Importing a manually created ZIP file

1. Create a ZIP file with the following structure:
   ```
   config.zip
   ├── DEFAULT_GROUP/
   │   └── application.yml
   └── meta_data
   ```
   Where `meta_data` contains:
   ```
   DEFAULT_GROUP|application.yml|
   ```

2. Go to Nacos Console → Configuration Management
3. Click "Import" button
4. Select the ZIP file
5. The import fails with error

### Case 2: Importing an exported ZIP file

1. Create a configuration in Nacos Console (e.g., `test.yml` in `DEFAULT_GROUP`)
2. Select the configuration and click "Export"
3. Try to import the exported ZIP file
4. The import fails with the same error

## Expected Behavior

The ZIP file should be imported successfully, and configurations should appear in the configuration list.

## Actual Behavior

Import fails with the following error response:

```json
{
  "code": 30000,
  "message": "Cannot invoke \"com.alibaba.nacos.config.server.utils.ZipUtils$ZipItem.getItemData()\" because \"metaDataItem\" is null",
  "data": null
}
```

## Environment

- **Nacos Version**: 3.1.2
- **Deployment Mode**: Standalone
- **Java Version**: JDK 17+
- **OS**: macOS / Linux

## Root Cause Analysis

After investigation, the issue appears to be:

1. **Export Bug**: When exporting configurations, the generated ZIP file does NOT include the `meta_data` file that is required for import. The exported ZIP only contains the configuration files in group directories.

2. **Import Bug**: The import function expects a `meta_data` file in the ZIP, but even when providing a correctly formatted `meta_data` file, the import still fails. This suggests there may be an issue in how `ZipUtils.java` parses or locates the `meta_data` file.

### Exported ZIP Structure (Current - Incorrect)
```
nacos_config_export.zip
└── DEFAULT_GROUP/
    └── config.yml    (no meta_data file!)
```

### Expected ZIP Structure (Correct)
```
nacos_config_export.zip
├── DEFAULT_GROUP/
│   └── config.yml
└── meta_data         (required!)
```

## Workaround

Use the API to create configurations individually:

```bash
curl -s "http://localhost:8080/v3/console/cs/config?accessToken=${TOKEN}&username=nacos" \
  -X 'POST' \
  -H 'Content-Type: application/x-www-form-urlencoded' \
  --data-urlencode 'dataId=application.yml' \
  --data-urlencode 'groupName=DEFAULT_GROUP' \
  --data-urlencode 'namespaceId=' \
  --data-urlencode 'content=<config_content>' \
  --data-urlencode 'type=yaml'
```

## Suggested Fix

1. Fix the export function to include `meta_data` file with proper format:
   ```
   GROUP|dataId|tenantId
   ```

2. Fix the import function (`ZipUtils.java`) to correctly locate and parse the `meta_data` file from the ZIP archive.

## Related Files

- `config/src/main/java/com/alibaba/nacos/config/server/utils/ZipUtils.java`
- `config/src/main/java/com/alibaba/nacos/config/server/controller/ConfigController.java`

## Additional Context

This bug makes the bulk configuration import/export feature completely unusable in Nacos 3.x, which is a critical feature for:
- Migrating configurations between environments
- Backup and restore operations
- Bulk configuration deployment

    17	package com.alibaba.nacos.config.server.utils;
    18	
    19	import com.alibaba.nacos.config.server.constant.Constants;
    20	import org.slf4j.Logger;
    21	import org.slf4j.LoggerFactory;
    22	
    23	import java.io.ByteArrayInputStream;
    24	import java.io.ByteArrayOutputStream;
    25	import java.io.IOException;
    26	import java.nio.charset.StandardCharsets;
    27	import java.util.ArrayList;
    28	import java.util.List;
    29	import java.util.zip.ZipEntry;
    30	import java.util.zip.ZipInputStream;
    31	import java.util.zip.ZipOutputStream;
    32	
    33	/**
    34	 * ZipUtils for import and export.
    35	 *
    36	 * @author klw
    37	 * @date 2019/5/14 16:59
    38	 */
    39	public class ZipUtils {
    40	    
    41	    private static final Logger LOGGER = LoggerFactory.getLogger(ZipUtils.class);
    42	    
    43	    public static class ZipItem {
    44	        
    45	        private String itemName;
    46	        
    47	        private String itemData;
    48	        
    49	        public ZipItem(String itemName, String itemData) {
    50	            this.itemName = itemName;
    51	            this.itemData = itemData;
    52	        }
    53	        
    54	        public String getItemName() {
    55	            return itemName;
    56	        }
    57	        
    58	        public void setItemName(String itemName) {
    59	            this.itemName = itemName;
    60	        }
    61	        
    62	        public String getItemData() {
    63	            return itemData;
    64	        }
    65	        
    66	        public void setItemData(String itemData) {
    67	            this.itemData = itemData;
    68	        }
    69	    }
    70	    
    71	    public static class UnZipResult {
    72	        
    73	        private List<ZipItem> zipItemList;
    74	        
    75	        private ZipItem metaDataItem;
    76	        
    77	        public UnZipResult(List<ZipItem> zipItemList, ZipItem metaDataItem) {
    78	            this.zipItemList = zipItemList;
    79	            this.metaDataItem = metaDataItem;
    80	        }
    81	        
    82	        public List<ZipItem> getZipItemList() {
    83	            return zipItemList;
    84	        }
    85	        
    86	        public void setZipItemList(List<ZipItem> zipItemList) {
    87	            this.zipItemList = zipItemList;
    88	        }
    89	        
    90	        public ZipItem getMetaDataItem() {
    91	            return metaDataItem;
    92	        }
    93	        
    94	        public void setMetaDataItem(ZipItem metaDataItem) {
    95	            this.metaDataItem = metaDataItem;
    96	        }
    97	    }
    98	    
    99	    /**
   100	     * zip method.
   101	     */
   102	    public static byte[] zip(List<ZipItem> source) {
   103	        byte[] result = null;
   104	        try (ByteArrayOutputStream byteOut = new ByteArrayOutputStream(); ZipOutputStream zipOut = new ZipOutputStream(
   105	                byteOut)) {
   106	            for (ZipItem item : source) {
   107	                zipOut.putNextEntry(new ZipEntry(item.getItemName()));
   108	                zipOut.write(item.getItemData().getBytes(StandardCharsets.UTF_8));
   109	            }
   110	            zipOut.flush();
   111	            zipOut.finish();
   112	            result = byteOut.toByteArray();
   113	        } catch (IOException e) {
   114	            LOGGER.error("an error occurred while compressing data.", e);
   115	        }
   116	        return result;
   117	    }
   118	    
   119	    /**
   120	     * unzip method.
   121	     */
   122	    public static UnZipResult unzip(byte[] source) {
   123	        List<ZipItem> itemList = new ArrayList<>();
   124	        ZipItem metaDataItem = null;
   125	        try (ZipInputStream zipIn = new ZipInputStream(new ByteArrayInputStream(source))) {
   126	            ZipEntry entry;
   127	            while ((entry = zipIn.getNextEntry()) != null) {
   128	                if (entry.isDirectory()) {
   129	                    continue;
   130	                }
   131	                try (ByteArrayOutputStream out = new ByteArrayOutputStream()) {
   132	                    byte[] buffer = new byte[1024];
   133	                    int offset;
   134	                    while ((offset = zipIn.read(buffer)) != -1) {
   135	                        out.write(buffer, 0, offset);
   136	                    }
   137	                    String entryName = entry.getName();
   138	                    if (metaDataItem == null && Constants.CONFIG_EXPORT_METADATA.equals(entryName)) {
   139	                        metaDataItem = new ZipItem(entryName, out.toString("UTF-8"));
   140	                        continue;
   141	                    }
   142	                    if (metaDataItem == null && Constants.CONFIG_EXPORT_METADATA_NEW.equals(entryName)) {
   143	                        metaDataItem = new ZipItem(entryName, out.toString("UTF-8"));
   144	                        continue;
   145	                    }
   146	                    itemList.add(new ZipItem(entryName, out.toString("UTF-8")));
   147	                } catch (IOException e) {
   148	                    LOGGER.error("unzip error", e);
   149	                }
   150	            }
   151	        } catch (IOException e) {
   152	            LOGGER.error("unzip error", e);
   153	        }
   154	        return new UnZipResult(itemList, metaDataItem);
   155	    }
   156	    
   157	}

   349	        String persistEncode = System.getenv(NACOS_PERSIST_ENCODE_KEY);
   350	        if (StringUtils.isBlank(persistEncode)) {
   351	            persistEncode = System.getProperty(NACOS_PERSIST_ENCODE_KEY);
   352	            if (StringUtils.isBlank(persistEncode)) {
   353	                persistEncode = DEFAULT_NACOS_ENCODE;
   354	            }
   355	        }
   356	        return persistEncode;
   357	    }

   139	    
   140	    private final ConfigMigrateService configMigrateService;
   141	    
   142	    /**
   143	     * Flag to indicate if the table `config_info_beta` exists, which means the old version of table schema is used.
   144	     */
   145	    private boolean oldTableVersion;
   146	    
   147	    public ConfigControllerV3(ConfigOperationService configOperationService,
   148	            ConfigInfoPersistService configInfoPersistService, ConfigDetailService configDetailService,
   149	            ConfigInfoGrayPersistService configInfoGrayPersistService,
   150	            ConfigInfoBetaPersistService configInfoBetaPersistService, NamespacePersistService namespacePersistService,
   151	            ConfigListenerStateDelegate configListenerStateDelegate, ConfigMigrateService configMigrateService) {
   152	        this.configOperationService = configOperationService;
   153	        this.configInfoPersistService = configInfoPersistService;
   154	        this.configDetailService = configDetailService;
   155	        this.configInfoGrayPersistService = configInfoGrayPersistService;
   156	        this.configInfoBetaPersistService = configInfoBetaPersistService;
   157	        this.namespacePersistService = namespacePersistService;
   158	        this.configListenerStateDelegate = configListenerStateDelegate;
   159	        this.configMigrateService = configMigrateService;
   160	        this.oldTableVersion = namespacePersistService.isExistTable("config_info_beta");
   161	    }
   162	    
   163	    /**
   164	     * Query configuration.
   165	     */
   166	    @GetMapping
   167	    @TpsControl(pointName = "ConfigQuery")
   168	    @Secured(action = ActionTypes.READ, signType = SignType.CONFIG, apiType = ApiType.ADMIN_API)
   169	    public Result<ConfigDetailInfo> getConfig(ConfigFormV3 configForm) throws NacosException {
   170	        configForm.validate();
   171	        // check namespaceId
   172	        String namespaceId = NamespaceUtil.processNamespaceParameter(configForm.getNamespaceId());
   173	        // check params
   174	        String dataId = configForm.getDataId();
   175	        String groupName = configForm.getGroupName();
   176	        ConfigAllInfo configAllInfo = configInfoPersistService.findConfigAllInfo(dataId, groupName, namespaceId);
   177	        if (Objects.isNull(configAllInfo)) {
   178	            throw new NacosApiException(NacosException.NOT_FOUND, ErrorCode.RESOURCE_NOT_FOUND,
   179	                    "Config not exist, please publish Config first.");
   180	        }
   181	        // decrypted
   182	        String encryptedDataKey = configAllInfo.getEncryptedDataKey();
   183	        Pair<String, String> pair = EncryptionHandler.decryptHandler(dataId, encryptedDataKey,
   184	                configAllInfo.getContent());
   185	        configAllInfo.setContent(pair.getSecond());
   186	        ConfigDetailInfo result = ResponseUtil.transferToConfigDetailInfo(configAllInfo);
   187	        return Result.success(result);
   188	    }
   189	    
   190	    /**
   191	     * Publish configuration.
   192	     */
   193	    @PostMapping
   194	    @TpsControl(pointName = "ConfigPublish")
   195	    @Secured(action = ActionTypes.WRITE, signType = SignType.CONFIG, apiType = ApiType.ADMIN_API)
   196	    public Result<Boolean> publishConfig(HttpServletRequest request, ConfigFormV3 configForm) throws NacosException {
   197	        // check required field
   198	        configForm.validateWithContent();
   199	        final boolean namespaceTransferred = NamespaceUtil.isNeedTransferNamespace(configForm.getNamespaceId());
   200	        configForm.setNamespaceId(NamespaceUtil.processNamespaceParameter(configForm.getNamespaceId()));
   201	        
   202	        // check param
   203	        ParamUtils.checkParam(configForm.getDataId(), configForm.getGroup(), "datumId", configForm.getContent());
   204	        ParamUtils.checkParamV2(configForm.getTag());
   205	        
   206	        if (StringUtils.isBlank(configForm.getSrcUser())) {
   207	            configForm.setSrcUser(RequestUtil.getSrcUserName(request));
   208	        }
   209	        
   210	        if (!ConfigType.isValidType(configForm.getType())) {
   211	            configForm.setType(ConfigType.getDefaultType().getType());
   212	        }
   213	        
   214	        String encryptedDataKeyFinal = configForm.getEncryptedDataKey();
   215	        if (StringUtils.isBlank(encryptedDataKeyFinal)) {
   216	            // encrypted
   217	            Pair<String, String> pair = EncryptionHandler.encryptHandler(configForm.getDataId(),
   218	                    configForm.getContent());
   219	            configForm.setContent(pair.getSecond());
   220	            encryptedDataKeyFinal = pair.getFirst();
   221	        }
   222	        
   223	        ConfigRequestInfo configRequestInfo = new ConfigRequestInfo();
   224	        configRequestInfo.setSrcIp(RequestUtil.getRemoteIp(request));
   225	        configRequestInfo.setRequestIpApp(RequestUtil.getAppName(request));
   226	        configRequestInfo.setBetaIps(request.getHeader("betaIps"));
   227	        configRequestInfo.setCasMd5(request.getHeader("casMd5"));
   228	        configRequestInfo.setNamespaceTransferred(namespaceTransferred);
   229	        
   230	        return Result.success(
   231	                configOperationService.publishConfig(configForm, configRequestInfo, encryptedDataKeyFinal));
   232	    }
   233	    
   234	    /**
   235	     * Publish config metadata result.
   236	     *
   237	     * @param request    the request
   238	     * @param configForm the config form
   239	     * @return the result
   240	     * @throws NacosException the nacos exception
   241	     */
   242	    @PutMapping("/metadata")
   243	    @Secured(action = ActionTypes.WRITE, signType = SignType.CONFIG, apiType = ApiType.ADMIN_API)
   244	    public Result<Boolean> publishConfigMetadata(HttpServletRequest request, ConfigFormV3 configForm)
   245	            throws NacosException {
   246	        configForm.validate();
   247	        String remoteIp = getRemoteIp(request);
   248	        String configTags = configForm.getConfigTags();
   249	        String description = configForm.getDesc();
   250	        String dataId = configForm.getDataId();
   251	        String group = configForm.getGroup();
   252	        String namespaceId = NamespaceUtil.processNamespaceParameter(configForm.getNamespaceId());
   253	        configInfoPersistService.updateConfigInfoMetadata(dataId, group, namespaceId, configTags, description);
   254	        configMigrateService.updateConfigMetadataMigrate(dataId, group, namespaceId, configTags, description);
   255	        final Timestamp time = TimeUtils.getCurrentTime();
   256	        ConfigTraceService.logPersistenceEvent(dataId, group, namespaceId, null, time.getTime(), remoteIp,
   257	                ConfigTraceService.PERSISTENCE_EVENT_METADATA, ConfigTraceService.PERSISTENCE_TYPE_PUB, null);
   258	        ConfigChangePublisher.notifyConfigChange(new ConfigDataChangeEvent(dataId, group, namespaceId, time.getTime()));
   259	        return Result.success(true);
   260	    }

   262	    /**
   263	     * Delete configuration.
   264	     */
   265	    @DeleteMapping
   266	    @Secured(action = ActionTypes.WRITE, signType = SignType.CONFIG, apiType = ApiType.ADMIN_API)
   267	    public Result<Boolean> deleteConfig(HttpServletRequest request, ConfigFormV3 configForm) throws NacosException {
   268	        configForm.validate();
   269	        // check namespaceId
   270	        String namespaceId = NamespaceUtil.processNamespaceParameter(configForm.getNamespaceId());
   271	        String tag = configForm.getTag();
   272	        ParamUtils.checkParamV2(tag);
   273	        
   274	        String clientIp = getRemoteIp(request);
   275	        String srcUser = RequestUtil.getSrcUserName(request);
   276	        
   277	        return Result.success(
   278	                configOperationService.deleteConfig(configForm.getDataId(), configForm.getGroupName(), namespaceId, tag,
   279	                        clientIp, srcUser, Constants.HTTP));
   280	    }
   281	    
   282	    /**
   283	     * Batch delete configuration by ids.
   284	     */
   285	    @DeleteMapping("/batch")
   286	    @Secured(action = ActionTypes.WRITE, signType = SignType.CONFIG, apiType = ApiType.ADMIN_API)
   287	    public Result<Boolean> deleteConfigs(HttpServletRequest request, @RequestParam(value = "ids") List<Long> ids) {
   288	        String clientIp = getRemoteIp(request);
   289	        String srcUser = RequestUtil.getSrcUserName(request);
   290	        try {
   291	            for (Long id : ids) {
   292	                ConfigInfo configInfo = configInfoPersistService.findConfigInfo(id);
   293	                if (configInfo == null) {
   294	                    LOGGER.warn("[deleteConfigs] configInfo is null, id: {}", id);
   295	                    continue;
   296	                }
   297	                configOperationService.deleteConfig(configInfo.getDataId(), configInfo.getGroup(),
   298	                        configInfo.getTenant(), null, clientIp, srcUser, Constants.HTTP);
   299	            }
   300	            return Result.success(true);
   301	        } catch (Exception e) {
   302	            LOGGER.error("delete configs based on the IDs list error, IDs: {}", ids, e);
   303	            return Result.failure(ErrorCode.SERVER_ERROR);
   304	        }
   305	    }

   310	    @GetMapping("/listener")
   311	    @Secured(action = ActionTypes.WRITE, signType = SignType.CONFIG, apiType = ApiType.ADMIN_API)
   312	    public Result<ConfigListenerInfo> getListeners(ConfigFormV3 configForm, AggregationForm aggregationForm)
   313	            throws Exception {

   315	        aggregationForm.validate();
   316	        String namespaceId = NamespaceUtil.processNamespaceParameter(configForm.getNamespaceId());

   318	                configListenerStateDelegate.getListenerState(configForm.getDataId(), configForm.getGroupName(),
   319	                        namespaceId, aggregationForm.isAggregation()));
   320	    }

   322	    /**
   323	     * List or Search config by config condition.
   324	     *
   325	     * <p>
   326	     * This API will entry the request into an queue to cache and do query limit. If API called with frequently or
   327	     * datasource is high performance and slow RT, The API will return {@code 503}. Can use
   328	     * `nacos.config.search.max_capacity` and `nacos.config.search.max_thread` to upper the limit of query. And use
   329	     * `nacos.config.search.wait_timeout` to control the waiting time of query.
   330	     * </p>
   331	     */
   332	    @GetMapping("/list")
   333	    @Secured(action = ActionTypes.READ, signType = SignType.CONFIG, apiType = ApiType.ADMIN_API)
   334	    @ExtractorManager.Extractor(httpExtractor = ConfigBlurSearchHttpParamExtractor.class)
   335	    public Result<Page<ConfigBasicInfo>> list(ConfigFormV3 configForm, PageForm pageForm, String configDetail,
   336	            @RequestParam(defaultValue = "blur") String search) throws NacosApiException {
   337	        configForm.blurSearchValidate();
   338	        pageForm.validate();
   339	        Map<String, Object> configAdvanceInfo = new HashMap<>(100);
   340	        if (StringUtils.isNotBlank(configForm.getAppName())) {
   341	            configAdvanceInfo.put("appName", configForm.getAppName());
   342	        }
   343	        if (StringUtils.isNotBlank(configForm.getConfigTags())) {
   344	            configAdvanceInfo.put("config_tags", configForm.getConfigTags());
   345	        }
   346	        if (StringUtils.isNotBlank(configForm.getType())) {
   347	            configAdvanceInfo.put(ParametersField.TYPES, configForm.getType());
   348	        }
   349	        if (StringUtils.isNotBlank(configDetail)) {
   350	            configAdvanceInfo.put("content", configDetail);
   351	        }
   352	        int pageNo = pageForm.getPageNo();
   353	        int pageSize = pageForm.getPageSize();
   354	        String namespaceId = NamespaceUtil.processNamespaceParameter(configForm.getNamespaceId());
   355	        String dataId = configForm.getDataId();
   356	        String groupName = configForm.getGroupName();
   357	        
   358	        Page<ConfigInfo> configInfoPage = configDetailService.findConfigInfoPage(search, pageNo, pageSize, dataId,
   359	                groupName, namespaceId, configAdvanceInfo);
   360	        Page<ConfigBasicInfo> result = new Page<>();
   361	        result.setTotalCount(configInfoPage.getTotalCount());
   362	        result.setPagesAvailable(configInfoPage.getPagesAvailable());
   363	        result.setPageNumber(configInfoPage.getPageNumber());
   364	        result.setPageItems(configInfoPage.getPageItems().stream().map(ResponseUtil::transferToConfigBasicInfo)
   365	                .collect(Collectors.toList()));
   366	        return Result.success(result);
   367	    }

   369	    /**
   370	     * Execute to remove beta operation.
   371	     */
   372	    @DeleteMapping("/beta")
   373	    @Secured(action = ActionTypes.WRITE, signType = SignType.CONFIG, apiType = ApiType.ADMIN_API)
   374	    public Result<Boolean> stopBeta(HttpServletRequest httpServletRequest, ConfigFormV3 configForm)
   375	            throws NacosApiException {
   376	        configForm.validate();
   377	        String remoteIp = getRemoteIp(httpServletRequest);
   378	        String requestIpApp = RequestUtil.getAppName(httpServletRequest);
   379	        String namespaceId = NamespaceUtil.processNamespaceParameter(configForm.getNamespaceId());
   380	        String dataId = configForm.getDataId();
   381	        String groupName = configForm.getGroupName();
   382	        try {
   383	            configInfoGrayPersistService.removeConfigInfoGray(dataId, groupName, namespaceId, BetaGrayRule.TYPE_BETA,
   384	                    remoteIp, RequestUtil.getSrcUserName(httpServletRequest));
   385	            configMigrateService.removeConfigInfoGrayMigrate(dataId, groupName, namespaceId, BetaGrayRule.TYPE_BETA,
   386	                    remoteIp, RequestUtil.getSrcUserName(httpServletRequest));
   387	        } catch (Throwable e) {
   388	            LOGGER.error("remove beta data error", e);
   389	            return Result.failure(ErrorCode.SERVER_ERROR.getCode(), "remove beta data error", false);
   390	        }
   391	        
   392	        ConfigTraceService.logPersistenceEvent(dataId, groupName, namespaceId, requestIpApp, System.currentTimeMillis(),
   393	                remoteIp, ConfigTraceService.PERSISTENCE_EVENT_BETA, ConfigTraceService.PERSISTENCE_TYPE_REMOVE, null);
   394	        if (PropertyUtil.isGrayCompatibleModel() && oldTableVersion) {
   395	            configInfoBetaPersistService.removeConfigInfo4Beta(dataId, groupName, namespaceId);
   396	        }
   397	        ConfigChangePublisher.notifyConfigChange(
   398	                new ConfigDataChangeEvent(dataId, groupName, namespaceId, BetaGrayRule.TYPE_BETA,
   399	                        System.currentTimeMillis()));
   400	        
   401	        return Result.success(true);
   402	    }

   404	    /**
   405	     * Execute to query beta operation.
   406	     */
   407	    @GetMapping("/beta")
   408	    @Secured(action = ActionTypes.READ, signType = SignType.CONFIG, apiType = ApiType.ADMIN_API)
   409	    public Result<ConfigGrayInfo> queryBeta(ConfigFormV3 configForm) throws NacosApiException {
   410	        configForm.validate();
   411	        String namespaceId = NamespaceUtil.processNamespaceParameter(configForm.getNamespaceId());
   412	        String dataId = configForm.getDataId();
   413	        String groupName = configForm.getGroupName();
   414	        ConfigInfoGrayWrapper beta4Gray = configInfoGrayPersistService.findConfigInfo4Gray(dataId, groupName,
   415	                namespaceId, "beta");
   416	        if (Objects.nonNull(beta4Gray)) {
   417	            String encryptedDataKey = beta4Gray.getEncryptedDataKey();
   418	            Pair<String, String> pair = EncryptionHandler.decryptHandler(dataId, encryptedDataKey,
   419	                    beta4Gray.getContent());
   420	            beta4Gray.setContent(pair.getSecond());
   421	            ConfigGrayInfo result = ResponseUtil.transferToConfigGrayInfo(beta4Gray);
   422	            return Result.success(result);
   423	        } else {
   424	            throw new NacosApiException(NacosException.NOT_FOUND, ErrorCode.RESOURCE_NOT_FOUND,
   425	                    "Config is not in beta.");
   426	        }
   427	    }
   428	    
   429	    /**
   430	     * Execute import and publish config operation.
   431	     */
   432	    @PostMapping("/import")
   433	    @Secured(action = ActionTypes.WRITE, signType = SignType.CONFIG, apiType = ApiType.ADMIN_API)
   434	    public Result<Map<String, Object>> importAndPublishConfig(HttpServletRequest request,
   435	            @RequestParam(value = "src_user", required = false) String srcUser,
   436	            @RequestParam(value = "namespaceId", required = false) String namespaceId,
   437	            @RequestParam(value = "policy", defaultValue = "ABORT") SameConfigPolicy policy, MultipartFile file)
   438	            throws NacosException {
   439	        Map<String, Object> failedData = new HashMap<>(4);
   440	        if (Objects.isNull(file)) {
   441	            return Result.failure(ErrorCode.DATA_EMPTY, failedData);
   442	        }
   443	        
   444	        namespaceId = NamespaceUtil.processNamespaceParameter(namespaceId);
   445	        if (StringUtils.isNotBlank(namespaceId) && !NamespaceUtil.isDefaultNamespaceId(namespaceId)
   446	                && namespacePersistService.tenantInfoCountByTenantId(namespaceId) <= 0) {
   447	            failedData.put("succCount", 0);
   448	            return Result.failure(ErrorCode.NAMESPACE_NOT_EXIST, failedData);
   449	        }
   450	        if (StringUtils.isBlank(srcUser)) {
   451	            srcUser = RequestUtil.getSrcUserName(request);
   452	        }
   453	        List<ConfigAllInfo> configInfoList = new ArrayList<>();
   454	        List<Map<String, String>> unrecognizedList = new ArrayList<>();
   455	        try {
   456	            ZipUtils.UnZipResult unziped = ZipUtils.unzip(file.getBytes());
   457	            Result<Map<String, Object>> errorResult = parseImportDataV2(srcUser, unziped, configInfoList,
   458	                    unrecognizedList, namespaceId);
   459	            if (errorResult != null) {
   460	                return errorResult;
   461	            }
   462	        } catch (IOException e) {
   463	            failedData.put("succCount", 0);
   464	            LOGGER.error("parsing data failed", e);
   465	            return Result.failure(ErrorCode.PARSING_DATA_FAILED, failedData);
   466	        }
   467	        
   468	        if (CollectionUtils.isEmpty(configInfoList)) {
   469	            failedData.put("succCount", 0);
   470	            return Result.failure(ErrorCode.DATA_EMPTY, failedData);
   471	        }
   472	        final String srcIp = RequestUtil.getRemoteIp(request);
   473	        String requestIpApp = RequestUtil.getAppName(request);
   474	        final Timestamp time = TimeUtils.getCurrentTime();
   475	        Map<String, Object> saveResult = configInfoPersistService.batchInsertOrUpdate(configInfoList, srcUser, srcIp,
   476	                null, policy);
   477	        for (ConfigInfo configInfo : configInfoList) {
   478	            ConfigChangePublisher.notifyConfigChange(
   479	                    new ConfigDataChangeEvent(configInfo.getDataId(), configInfo.getGroup(), configInfo.getTenant(),
   480	                            time.getTime()));
   481	            ConfigTraceService.logPersistenceEvent(configInfo.getDataId(), configInfo.getGroup(),
   482	                    configInfo.getTenant(), requestIpApp, time.getTime(), InetUtils.getSelfIP(),
   483	                    ConfigTraceService.PERSISTENCE_EVENT, ConfigTraceService.PERSISTENCE_TYPE_PUB,
   484	                    configInfo.getContent());
   485	        }
   486	        // unrecognizedCount
   487	        if (!unrecognizedList.isEmpty()) {
   488	            saveResult.put("unrecognizedCount", unrecognizedList.size());
   489	            saveResult.put("unrecognizedData", unrecognizedList);
   490	        }
   491	        
   492	        return Result.success(saveResult);
   493	    }
   494	    
   495	    /**
   496	     * Import config add .metadata.yml file.
   497	     */
   498	    private Result<Map<String, Object>> parseImportDataV2(String srcUser, ZipUtils.UnZipResult unziped,
   499	            List<ConfigAllInfo> configInfoList, List<Map<String, String>> unrecognizedList, String namespaceId) {
   500	        ZipUtils.ZipItem metaDataItem = unziped.getMetaDataItem();
   501	        String metaData = metaDataItem.getItemData();
   502	        Map<String, Object> failedData = new HashMap<>(4);
   503	        
   504	        ConfigMetadata configMetadata = YamlParserUtil.loadObject(metaData, ConfigMetadata.class);
   505	        if (configMetadata == null || CollectionUtils.isEmpty(configMetadata.getMetadata())) {
   506	            failedData.put("succCount", 0);
   507	            return Result.failure(ErrorCode.METADATA_ILLEGAL, failedData);
   508	        }
   509	        List<ConfigMetadata.ConfigExportItem> configExportItems = configMetadata.getMetadata();
   510	        // check config metadata
   511	        for (ConfigMetadata.ConfigExportItem configExportItem : configExportItems) {
   512	            if (StringUtils.isBlank(configExportItem.getDataId()) || StringUtils.isBlank(configExportItem.getGroup())
   513	                    || StringUtils.isBlank(configExportItem.getType())) {
   514	                failedData.put("succCount", 0);
   515	                return Result.failure(ErrorCode.METADATA_ILLEGAL, failedData);
   516	            }
   517	        }
   518	        
   519	        List<ZipUtils.ZipItem> zipItemList = unziped.getZipItemList();
   520	        Set<String> metaDataKeys = configExportItems.stream()
   521	                .map(metaItem -> GroupKey.getKey(metaItem.getDataId(), metaItem.getGroup()))
   522	                .collect(Collectors.toSet());
   523	        
   524	        Map<String, String> configContentMap = new HashMap<>(zipItemList.size());
   525	        int itemNameLength = 2;
   526	        zipItemList.forEach(item -> {
   527	            String itemName = item.getItemName();
   528	            String[] groupAdnDataId = itemName.split(Constants.CONFIG_EXPORT_ITEM_FILE_SEPARATOR);
   529	            if (groupAdnDataId.length != itemNameLength) {
   530	                Map<String, String> unrecognizedItem = new HashMap<>(2);
   531	                unrecognizedItem.put("itemName", item.getItemName());
   532	                unrecognizedList.add(unrecognizedItem);
   533	                return;
   534	            }
   535	            
   536	            String group = groupAdnDataId[0];
   537	            String dataId = groupAdnDataId[1];
   538	            String key = GroupKey.getKey(dataId, group);
   539	            // metadata does not contain config file
   540	            if (!metaDataKeys.contains(key)) {
   541	                Map<String, String> unrecognizedItem = new HashMap<>(2);
   542	                unrecognizedItem.put("itemName", "Item not found in metadata: " + item.getItemName());
   543	                unrecognizedList.add(unrecognizedItem);
   544	                return;
   545	            }
   546	            String itemData = item.getItemData();
   547	            configContentMap.put(key, itemData);
   548	        });
   549	        
   550	        for (ConfigMetadata.ConfigExportItem configExportItem : configExportItems) {
   551	            String dataId = configExportItem.getDataId();
   552	            String group = configExportItem.getGroup();
   553	            String content = configContentMap.get(GroupKey.getKey(dataId, group));
   554	            // config file not in metadata
   555	            if (content == null) {
   556	                Map<String, String> unrecognizedItem = new HashMap<>(2);
   557	                unrecognizedItem.put("itemName", "Item not found in file: " + group + "/" + dataId);
   558	                unrecognizedList.add(unrecognizedItem);
   559	                continue;
   560	            }
   561	            // encrypted
   562	            Pair<String, String> pair = EncryptionHandler.encryptHandler(dataId, content);
   563	            content = pair.getSecond();
   564	            
   565	            ConfigAllInfo ci = new ConfigAllInfo();
   566	            ci.setGroup(group);
   567	            ci.setDataId(dataId);
   568	            ci.setContent(content);
   569	            ci.setType(configExportItem.getType());
   570	            ci.setDesc(configExportItem.getDesc());
   571	            ci.setAppName(configExportItem.getAppName());
   572	            ci.setTenant(namespaceId);
   573	            ci.setEncryptedDataKey(pair.getFirst());
   574	            ci.setCreateUser(srcUser);
   575	            configInfoList.add(ci);
   576	        }
   577	        
   578	        return null;
   579	    }
   580	    
   581	    /**
   582	     * Export config add metadata.yml file record config metadata.
   583	     */
   584	    @GetMapping("/export")
   585	    @Secured(action = ActionTypes.READ, signType = SignType.CONFIG, apiType = ApiType.ADMIN_API)
   586	    public ResponseEntity<byte[]> exportConfig(ConfigFormV3 configForm,
   587	            @RequestParam(value = "ids", required = false) List<Long> ids) throws NacosApiException {
   588	        configForm.blurSearchValidate();
   589	        ids.removeAll(Collections.singleton(null));
   590	        String namespaceId = NamespaceUtil.processNamespaceParameter(configForm.getNamespaceId());
   591	        List<ConfigAllInfo> dataList = configInfoPersistService.findAllConfigInfo4Export(configForm.getDataId(),
   592	                configForm.getGroupName(), namespaceId, configForm.getAppName(), ids);
   593	        List<ZipUtils.ZipItem> zipItemList = new ArrayList<>();
   594	        List<ConfigMetadata.ConfigExportItem> configMetadataItems = new ArrayList<>();
   595	        for (ConfigAllInfo ci : dataList) {
   596	            ConfigMetadata.ConfigExportItem configMetadataItem = new ConfigMetadata.ConfigExportItem();
   597	            configMetadataItem.setAppName(ci.getAppName());
   598	            configMetadataItem.setDataId(ci.getDataId());
   599	            configMetadataItem.setDesc(ci.getDesc());
   600	            configMetadataItem.setGroup(ci.getGroup());
   601	            configMetadataItem.setType(ci.getType());
   602	            configMetadataItems.add(configMetadataItem);
   603	            Pair<String, String> pair = EncryptionHandler.decryptHandler(ci.getDataId(), ci.getEncryptedDataKey(),
   604	                    ci.getContent());
   605	            String itemName = ci.getGroup() + Constants.CONFIG_EXPORT_ITEM_FILE_SEPARATOR + ci.getDataId();
   606	            zipItemList.add(new ZipUtils.ZipItem(itemName, pair.getSecond()));
   607	        }
   608	        ConfigMetadata configMetadata = new ConfigMetadata();
   609	        configMetadata.setMetadata(configMetadataItems);
   610	        zipItemList.add(
   611	                new ZipUtils.ZipItem(Constants.CONFIG_EXPORT_METADATA_NEW, YamlParserUtil.dumpObject(configMetadata)));
   612	        HttpHeaders headers = new HttpHeaders();
   613	        String fileName =
   614	                EXPORT_CONFIG_FILE_NAME + DateFormatUtils.format(new Date(), EXPORT_CONFIG_FILE_NAME_DATE_FORMAT)
   615	                        + EXPORT_CONFIG_FILE_NAME_EXT;
   616	        headers.add("Content-Disposition", "attachment;filename=" + fileName);
   617	        
   618	        return new ResponseEntity<>(ZipUtils.zip(zipItemList), headers, HttpStatus.OK);
   619	    }
   620	    
   621	    /**
   622	     * Execute clone config operation.
   623	     */
   624	    @PostMapping("/clone")
   625	    @Secured(action = ActionTypes.WRITE, signType = SignType.CONFIG, apiType = ApiType.CONSOLE_API)
   626	    public Result<Map<String, Object>> cloneConfig(HttpServletRequest request,
   627	            @RequestParam(value = "src_user", required = false) String srcUser,
   628	            @RequestParam(value = "namespaceId") String namespaceId, @RequestBody List<ConfigCloneInfo> cloneInfos,
   629	            @RequestParam(value = "policy", defaultValue = "ABORT") SameConfigPolicy policy) throws NacosException {
   630	        Map<String, Object> failedData = new HashMap<>(4);
   631	        if (CollectionUtils.isEmpty(cloneInfos)) {
   632	            failedData.put("succCount", 0);
   633	            return Result.failure(ErrorCode.NO_SELECTED_CONFIG, failedData);
   634	        }
   635	        cloneInfos.removeAll(Collections.singleton(null));
   636	        
   637	        namespaceId = NamespaceUtil.processNamespaceParameter(namespaceId);
   638	        if (StringUtils.isNotBlank(namespaceId) && !NamespaceUtil.isDefaultNamespaceId(namespaceId)
   639	                && namespacePersistService.tenantInfoCountByTenantId(namespaceId) <= 0) {
   640	            failedData.put("succCount", 0);
   641	            return Result.failure(ErrorCode.NAMESPACE_NOT_EXIST, failedData);
   642	        }
   643	        
   644	        List<Long> idList = new ArrayList<>(cloneInfos.size());
   645	        Map<Long, ConfigCloneInfo> configBeansMap = cloneInfos.stream()
   646	                .collect(Collectors.toMap(ConfigCloneInfo::getConfigId, cfg -> {
   647	                    idList.add(cfg.getConfigId());
   648	                    return cfg;
   649	                }, (k1, k2) -> k1));
   650	        
   651	        List<ConfigAllInfo> queryedDataList = configInfoPersistService.findAllConfigInfo4Export(null, null, null, null,
   652	                idList);
   653	        
   654	        if (queryedDataList == null || queryedDataList.isEmpty()) {
   655	            failedData.put("succCount", 0);
   656	            return Result.failure(ErrorCode.DATA_EMPTY, failedData);
   657	        }
   658	        
   659	        List<ConfigAllInfo> configInfoList4Clone = new ArrayList<>(queryedDataList.size());
   660	        
   661	        for (ConfigAllInfo ci : queryedDataList) {
   662	            ConfigCloneInfo paramBean = configBeansMap.get(ci.getId());
   663	            ConfigAllInfo ci4save = new ConfigAllInfo();
   664	            ci4save.setTenant(namespaceId);
   665	            ci4save.setType(ci.getType());
   666	            ci4save.setGroup((paramBean != null && StringUtils.isNotBlank(paramBean.getTargetGroupName()))
   667	                    ? paramBean.getTargetGroupName() : ci.getGroup());
   668	            ci4save.setDataId((paramBean != null && StringUtils.isNotBlank(paramBean.getTargetDataId()))
   669	                    ? paramBean.getTargetDataId() : ci.getDataId());
   670	            ci4save.setContent(ci.getContent());
   671	            if (StringUtils.isNotBlank(ci.getAppName())) {
   672	                ci4save.setAppName(ci.getAppName());
   673	            }
   674	            ci4save.setDesc(ci.getDesc());
   675	            ci4save.setEncryptedDataKey(
   676	                    ci.getEncryptedDataKey() == null ? StringUtils.EMPTY : ci.getEncryptedDataKey());
   677	            configInfoList4Clone.add(ci4save);
   678	        }
   679	        if (StringUtils.isBlank(srcUser)) {
   680	            srcUser = RequestUtil.getSrcUserName(request);
   681	        }
   682	        final String srcIp = getRemoteIp(request);
   683	        String requestIpApp = RequestUtil.getAppName(request);
   684	        final Timestamp time = TimeUtils.getCurrentTime();
   685	        Map<String, Object> saveResult = configInfoPersistService.batchInsertOrUpdate(configInfoList4Clone, srcUser,
   686	                srcIp, null, policy);
   687	        for (ConfigInfo configInfo : configInfoList4Clone) {
   688	            ConfigChangePublisher.notifyConfigChange(
   689	                    new ConfigDataChangeEvent(configInfo.getDataId(), configInfo.getGroup(), configInfo.getTenant(),
   690	                            time.getTime()));
   691	            ConfigTraceService.logPersistenceEvent(configInfo.getDataId(), configInfo.getGroup(),
   692	                    configInfo.getTenant(), requestIpApp, time.getTime(), InetUtils.getSelfIP(),
   693	                    ConfigTraceService.PERSISTENCE_EVENT, ConfigTraceService.PERSISTENCE_TYPE_PUB,
   694	                    configInfo.getContent());
   695	        }
   696	        
   697	        return Result.success(saveResult);
   698	    }
   699	}

    96	    public Result<ConfigDetailInfo> getConfigDetail(ConfigFormV3 configForm) throws NacosException {

   104	    /**
   105	     * Add or update configuration.
   106	     *
   107	     * @param request    HTTP servlet request.
   108	     * @param configForm Configuration form.
   109	     * @return Result containing success status.
   110	     * @throws NacosException If a Nacos-specific error occurs.
   111	     */
   112	    @PostMapping()
   113	    @Secured(action = ActionTypes.WRITE, signType = SignType.CONFIG, apiType = ApiType.CONSOLE_API)
   114	    public Result<Boolean> publishConfig(HttpServletRequest request, ConfigFormV3 configForm) throws NacosException {
   115	        // check required field
   116	        configForm.validateWithContent();
   117	        final boolean namespaceTransferred = NamespaceUtil.isNeedTransferNamespace(configForm.getNamespaceId());
   118	        configForm.setNamespaceId(NamespaceUtil.processNamespaceParameter(configForm.getNamespaceId()));
   119	        
   120	        // check param
   121	        ParamUtils.checkParam(configForm.getDataId(), configForm.getGroup(), "datumId", configForm.getContent());
   122	        ParamUtils.checkParamV2(configForm.getTag());
   123	        
   124	        if (StringUtils.isBlank(configForm.getSrcUser())) {
   125	            configForm.setSrcUser(RequestUtil.getSrcUserName(request));
   126	        }
   127	        if (!ConfigType.isValidType(configForm.getType())) {
   128	            configForm.setType(ConfigType.getDefaultType().getType());
   129	        }
   130	        
   131	        ConfigRequestInfo configRequestInfo = new ConfigRequestInfo();
   132	        configRequestInfo.setSrcIp(RequestUtil.getRemoteIp(request));
   133	        configRequestInfo.setRequestIpApp(RequestUtil.getAppName(request));
   134	        configRequestInfo.setBetaIps(request.getHeader("betaIps"));
   135	        configRequestInfo.setCasMd5(request.getHeader("casMd5"));
   136	        configRequestInfo.setNamespaceTransferred(namespaceTransferred);
   137	        
   138	        return Result.success(configProxy.publishConfig(configForm, configRequestInfo));
   139	    }

   319	    /**

   327	     * @return Result containing a map of the import status.
   328	     * @throws NacosException If a Nacos-specific error occurs.

   330	    @PostMapping("/import")
   331	    @Secured(action = ActionTypes.WRITE, signType = SignType.CONFIG, apiType = ApiType.CONSOLE_API)
   332	    public Result<Map<String, Object>> importAndPublishConfig(HttpServletRequest request,
   333	            @RequestParam(required = false) String srcUser,
   334	            @RequestParam(value = "namespaceId", required = false) String namespaceId,
   335	            @RequestParam(value = "policy", defaultValue = "ABORT") SameConfigPolicy policy, MultipartFile file)
   336	            throws NacosException {
   337	        namespaceId = NamespaceUtil.processNamespaceParameter(namespaceId);
   338	        
   339	        if (StringUtils.isBlank(srcUser)) {
   340	            srcUser = RequestUtil.getSrcUserName(request);
   341	        }
   342	        final String srcIp = RequestUtil.getRemoteIp(request);
   343	        String requestIpApp = RequestUtil.getAppName(request);
   344	        
   345	        return configProxy.importAndPublishConfig(srcUser, namespaceId, policy, file, srcIp, requestIpApp);
   346	    }
   347	    
   348	    /**
   349	     * Clone configuration.
   350	     *
   351	     * @param request         HTTP servlet request.
   352	     * @param srcUser         Source user string value.
   353	     * @param namespaceId     Namespace string value.
   354	     * @param configBeansList List of configuration beans.
   355	     * @param policy          Policy model.
   356	     * @return Result containing a map of the clone status.
   357	     * @throws NacosException If a Nacos-specific error occurs.
   358	     */
   359	    @PostMapping("/clone")
   360	    @Secured(action = ActionTypes.WRITE, signType = SignType.CONFIG, apiType = ApiType.CONSOLE_API, tags = {
   361	            com.alibaba.nacos.plugin.auth.constant.Constants.Tag.SECURED_SPECIAL_TAGS})
   362	    public Result<Map<String, Object>> cloneConfig(HttpServletRequest request,
   363	            @RequestParam(required = false) String srcUser,
   364	            @RequestParam(value = "targetNamespaceId") String namespaceId,
   365	            @RequestBody List<SameNamespaceCloneConfigBean> configBeansList,
   366	            @RequestParam(value = "policy", defaultValue = "ABORT") SameConfigPolicy policy) throws NacosException {
   367	        configBeansList.removeAll(Collections.singleton(null));
   368	        namespaceId = NamespaceUtil.processNamespaceParameter(namespaceId);
   369	        if (StringUtils.isBlank(srcUser)) {
   370	            srcUser = RequestUtil.getSrcUserName(request);
   371	        }
   372	        final String srcIp = RequestUtil.getRemoteIp(request);
   373	        String requestIpApp = RequestUtil.getAppName(request);
   374	        
   375	        return configProxy.cloneConfig(srcUser, namespaceId, configBeansList, policy, srcIp, requestIpApp);
   376	    }
   377	    
   378	    /**
   379	     * Execute to remove beta operation.
   380	     *
   381	     * @param httpServletRequest HTTP request containing client details.
   382	     * @param configForm         config form
   383	     * @return Result indicating the outcome of the operation.
   384	     * @throws NacosException If a Nacos-specific error occurs.
   385	     */
   386	    @DeleteMapping("/beta")
   387	    @Secured(action = ActionTypes.WRITE, signType = SignType.CONFIG)
   388	    public Result<Boolean> stopBeta(HttpServletRequest httpServletRequest, ConfigFormV3 configForm)
   389	            throws NacosException {
   390	        configForm.validate();
   391	        String remoteIp = getRemoteIp(httpServletRequest);
   392	        String requestIpApp = RequestUtil.getAppName(httpServletRequest);
   393	        String dataId = configForm.getDataId();
   394	        String groupName = configForm.getGroupName();
   395	        String namespaceId = NamespaceUtil.processNamespaceParameter(configForm.getNamespaceId());
   396	        String srcUser = RequestUtil.getSrcUserName(httpServletRequest);
   397	        boolean success = configProxy.removeBetaConfig(dataId, groupName, namespaceId, remoteIp, requestIpApp, srcUser);
   398	        if (!success) {
   399	            return Result.failure(HttpStatus.INTERNAL_SERVER_ERROR.value(),
   400	                    HttpStatus.INTERNAL_SERVER_ERROR.getReasonPhrase(), false);
   401	        }
   402	        return Result.success(true);
   403	    }
   404	    
   405	    /**
   406	     * Execute to query beta operation.
   407	     *
   408	     * @param configForm config form
   409	     * @return Result containing the ConfigInfo4Beta details.
   410	     * @throws NacosException If a Nacos-specific error occurs.
   411	     */
   412	    @GetMapping("/beta")
   413	    @Secured(action = ActionTypes.READ, signType = SignType.CONFIG)
   414	    public Result<ConfigGrayInfo> queryBeta(ConfigFormV3 configForm) throws NacosException {
   415	        configForm.validate();
   416	        String dataId = configForm.getDataId();
   417	        String groupName = configForm.getGroupName();
   418	        String namespaceId = NamespaceUtil.processNamespaceParameter(configForm.getNamespaceId());
   419	        return Result.success(configProxy.queryBetaConfig(dataId, groupName, namespaceId));
   420	    }
   421	    
   422	}

    17	package com.alibaba.nacos.config.server.utils;
    18	
    19	import com.alibaba.nacos.api.exception.NacosException;
    20	import com.alibaba.nacos.api.exception.runtime.NacosRuntimeException;
    21	import com.alibaba.nacos.common.utils.CollectionUtils;
    22	import com.alibaba.nacos.config.server.model.ConfigMetadata;
    23	import org.yaml.snakeyaml.DumperOptions;
    24	import org.yaml.snakeyaml.LoaderOptions;
    25	import org.yaml.snakeyaml.constructor.AbstractConstruct;
    26	import org.yaml.snakeyaml.constructor.SafeConstructor;
    27	import org.yaml.snakeyaml.introspector.Property;
    28	import org.yaml.snakeyaml.Yaml;
    29	import org.yaml.snakeyaml.nodes.MappingNode;
    30	import org.yaml.snakeyaml.nodes.Node;
    31	import org.yaml.snakeyaml.nodes.NodeTuple;
    32	import org.yaml.snakeyaml.nodes.ScalarNode;
    33	import org.yaml.snakeyaml.nodes.SequenceNode;
    34	import org.yaml.snakeyaml.nodes.Tag;
    35	import org.yaml.snakeyaml.representer.Representer;
    36	
    37	import java.util.HashMap;
    38	import java.util.List;
    39	import java.util.Map;
    40	import java.util.stream.Collectors;
    41	
    42	/**
    43	 * YamlParserUtil.
    44	 *
    45	 * @author Nacos
    46	 */
    47	public class YamlParserUtil {
    48	    
    49	    /**
    50	     * Serialize a Java object into a YAML string.
    51	     *
    52	     * @param object Java object.
    53	     * @return YAML string.
    54	     */
    55	    public static String dumpObject(Object object) {
    56	        return new Yaml(new YamlParserConstructor(), new CustomRepresenter()).dumpAsMap(object);
    57	    }
    58	    
    59	    /**
    60	     * Parse YAML String and produce the corresponding Java object (Standard Java classes and in YamlParserConstructor
    61	     * specified Construct).
    62	     *
    63	     * @param content YAML String
    64	     * @param type    Java object.
    65	     * @param <T>     Java object type.
    66	     * @return Java object.
    67	     */
    68	    public static <T> T loadObject(String content, Class<T> type) {
    69	        return new Yaml(new YamlParserConstructor(), new CustomRepresenter()).loadAs(content, type);
    70	    }
    71	    
    72	    public static class YamlParserConstructor extends SafeConstructor {
    73	        
    74	        public static final Tag CONFIG_METADATA_TAG = new Tag(ConfigMetadata.class);
    75	        
    76	        public YamlParserConstructor() {
    77	            super(new LoaderOptions());
    78	            yamlConstructors.put(CONFIG_METADATA_TAG, new ConstructYamlConfigMetadata());
    79	        }
    80	    }
    81	    
    82	    public static class CustomRepresenter extends Representer {
    83	    
    84	        public CustomRepresenter() {
    85	            super(new DumperOptions());
    86	        }
    87	    
    88	        @Override
    89	        protected NodeTuple representJavaBeanProperty(Object javaBean, Property property, Object propertyValue,
    90	                Tag customTag) {
    91	            if (propertyValue == null) {
    92	                return null;
    93	            } else {
    94	                return super.representJavaBeanProperty(javaBean, property, propertyValue, customTag);
    95	            }
    96	        }
    97	    }
    98	    
    99	    public static class ConstructYamlConfigMetadata extends AbstractConstruct {
   100	        
   101	        @Override
   102	        public Object construct(Node node) {
   103	            if (!YamlParserConstructor.CONFIG_METADATA_TAG.getValue().equals(node.getTag().getValue())) {
   104	                throw new NacosRuntimeException(NacosException.INVALID_PARAM,
   105	                        "could not determine a constructor for the tag " + node.getTag() + node.getStartMark());
   106	            }
   107	            
   108	            MappingNode mNode = (MappingNode) node;
   109	            List<NodeTuple> value = mNode.getValue();
   110	            if (CollectionUtils.isEmpty(value)) {
   111	                return null;
   112	            }
   113	            NodeTuple nodeTuple = value.get(0);
   114	            ConfigMetadata configMetadata = new ConfigMetadata();
   115	            SequenceNode sequenceNode = (SequenceNode) nodeTuple.getValueNode();
   116	            if (CollectionUtils.isEmpty(sequenceNode.getValue())) {
   117	                return configMetadata;
   118	            }
   119	            
   120	            List<ConfigMetadata.ConfigExportItem> exportItems = sequenceNode.getValue().stream().map(itemValue -> {
   121	                ConfigMetadata.ConfigExportItem configExportItem = new ConfigMetadata.ConfigExportItem();
   122	                MappingNode itemMap = (MappingNode) itemValue;
   123	                List<NodeTuple> propertyValues = itemMap.getValue();
   124	                Map<String, String> metadataMap = new HashMap<>(propertyValues.size());
   125	                propertyValues.forEach(metadata -> {
   126	                    ScalarNode keyNode = (ScalarNode) metadata.getKeyNode();
   127	                    ScalarNode valueNode = (ScalarNode) metadata.getValueNode();
   128	                    metadataMap.put(keyNode.getValue(), valueNode.getValue());
   129	                });
   130	                configExportItem.setDataId(metadataMap.get("dataId"));
   131	                configExportItem.setGroup(metadataMap.get("group"));
   132	                configExportItem.setType(metadataMap.get("type"));
   133	                configExportItem.setDesc(metadataMap.get("desc"));
   134	                configExportItem.setAppName(metadataMap.get("appName"));
   135	                configExportItem.setConfigTags(metadataMap.get("configTags"));
   136	                return configExportItem;
   137	            }).collect(Collectors.toList());
   138	            
   139	            configMetadata.setMetadata(exportItems);
   140	            return configMetadata;
   141	        }
   142	    }
   143	    
   144	}

2026-05-30 04:08:28,645 - INFO - swea-agent-alibaba__nacos-14917 - 💭 THOUGHT
Now I have a thorough understanding of the issue. Let me analyze:

**Problem Analysis:**

1. **Export**: The `exportConfig` method in `ConfigControllerV3` (line 584-619) creates a `.metadata.yml` file (using `Constants.CONFIG_EXPORT_METADATA_NEW = ".metadata.yml"`) and adds it as a zip item. The export looks correct.

2. **Import**: The `unzip` method in `ZipUtils.java` (line 122-155) looks for `Constants.CONFIG_EXPORT_METADATA` (`.meta.yml`) or `Constants.CONFIG_EXPORT_METADATA_NEW` (`.metadata.yml`). 

   The bug is in the `unzip` method: it checks `if (metaDataItem == null && Constants.CONFIG_EXPORT_METADATA.equals(entryName))` and `if (metaDataItem == null && Constants.CONFIG_EXPORT_METADATA_NEW.equals(entryName))`. But `entryName` at this point is the full path from the zip entry (e.g., `.metadata.yml`). Since the entry name is just the filename (not a path), this should work.

   Wait, let me re-examine. The PR description says the error is:
   ```
   "Cannot invoke \"com.alibaba.nacos.config.server.utils.ZipUtils$ZipItem.getItemData()\" because \"metaDataItem\" is null"
   ```
   
   This means `metaDataItem` is null after unzipping. Looking at the `unzip` method more carefully:

   ```java
   String entryName = entry.getName();
   if (metaDataItem == null && Constants.CONFIG_EXPORT_METADATA.equals(entryName)) {
       metaDataItem = new ZipItem(entryName, out.toString("UTF-8"));
       continue;
   }
   if (metaDataItem == null && Constants.CONFIG_EXPORT_METADATA_NEW.equals(entryName)) {
       metaDataItem = new ZipItem(entryName, out.toString("UTF-8"));
       continue;
   }
   ```

   The constants are:
   - `CONFIG_EXPORT_METADATA = ".meta.yml"`
   - `CONFIG_EXPORT_METADATA_NEW = ".metadata.yml"`

   But wait - in the import endpoint, `parseImportDataV2` (line 498-579) is called which expects `metaDataItem` to be non-null and uses it to parse YAML metadata. 

   However, looking at the PR description, the "Case 1" uses a simple text file `meta_data` with format `DEFAULT_GROUP|application.yml|`. This is the OLD format which is no longer used (the new format uses `.metadata.yml` YAML file).

   But the real issue is: even when exporting and re-importing, it fails. Let me check more carefully...

   Actually, looking at the export code again:
   ```java
   String itemName = ci.getGroup() + Constants.CONFIG_EXPORT_ITEM_FILE_SEPARATOR + ci.getDataId();
   ```
   
   This creates entries like `DEFAULT_GROUP/application.yml`. The `/` is a path separator. In a ZIP file, this would create a directory structure. When you unzip, the entry name would be `DEFAULT_GROUP/application.yml`.

   But wait, the `meta_data` file is added as:
   ```java
   new ZipUtils.ZipItem(Constants.CONFIG_EXPORT_METADATA_NEW, YamlParserUtil.dumpObject(configMetadata))
   ```
   
   So it's added as `.metadata.yml` (without any directory prefix).

   Now in `unzip`:
   ```java
   if (entry.isDirectory()) {
       continue;
   }
   ```
   
   The issue might be with directories! When you zip entries like `DEFAULT_GROUP/application.yml`, the ZIP may contain a directory entry `DEFAULT_GROUP/` that gets skipped. But the file entries should be fine.

   Let me write a test script to reproduce the issue.

🎬 ACTION
cd /testbed && cat > /tmp/ReproZipTest.java << 'EOF'
import com.alibaba.nacos.config.server.utils.ZipUtils;
import java.io.*;
import java.nio.file.*;
import java.util.*;
import java.util.zip.*;

public class ReproduceZipTest {
    public static void main(String[] args) throws Exception {
        System.out.println("=== Test 1: zip/unzip with meta_data (simple text format) ===");
        testSimpleMetaData();
        
        System.out.println("\n=== Test 2: zip/unzip with .metadata.yml (YAML format) ===");
        testYamlMetaData();
        
        System.out.println("\n=== Test 3: unzip of a manually created ZIP (simulating console export) ===");
        testManualZip();
    }
    
    static void testSimpleMetaData() {
        List<ZipUtils.ZipItem> items = new ArrayList<>();
        items.add(new ZipUtils.ZipItem("DEFAULT_GROUP/application.yml", "some: content"));
        items.add(new ZipUtils.ZipItem(".meta.yml", "metadata content"));
        
        byte[] zip = ZipUtils.zip(items);
        System.out.println("Zipped: " + zip.length + " bytes");
        
        ZipUtils.UnZipResult result = ZipUtils.unzip(zip);
        System.out.println("MetaDataItem: " + (result.getMetaDataItem() != null ? result.getMetaDataItem().getItemName() : "NULL"));
        System.out.println("ZipItemList size: " + result.getZipItemList().size());
        for (ZipUtils.ZipItem item : result.getZipItemList()) {
            System.out.println("  - " + item.getItemName());
        }
    }
    
    static void testYamlMetaData() {
        List<ZipUtils.ZipItem> items = new ArrayList<>();
        items.add(new ZipUtils.ZipItem("DEFAULT_GROUP/application.yml", "some: content"));
        items.add(new ZipUtils.ZipItem(".metadata.yml", "metadata content"));
        
        byte[] zip = ZipUtils.zip(items);
        System.out.println("Zipped: " + zip.length + " bytes");
        
        ZipUtils.UnZipResult result = ZipUtils.unzip(zip);
        System.out.println("MetaDataItem: " + (result.getMetaDataItem() != null ? result.getMetaDataItem().getItemName() : "NULL"));
        System.out.println("ZipItemList size: " + result.getZipItemList().size());
        for (ZipUtils.ZipItem item : result.getZipItemList()) {
            System.out.println("  - " + item.getItemName());
        }
    }
    
    static void testManualZip() throws Exception {
        // Create a ZIP manually like the console export does
        ByteArrayOutputStream baos = new ByteArrayOutputStream();
        ZipOutputStream zos = new ZipOutputStream(baos);
        
        // Add a config file entry
        zos.putNextEntry(new ZipEntry("DEFAULT_GROUP/"));
        zos.closeEntry();
        
        zos.putNextEntry(new ZipEntry("DEFAULT_GROUP/application.yml"));
        zos.write("some: content".getBytes("UTF-8"));
        zos.closeEntry();
        
        // Add metadata
        zos.putNextEntry(new ZipEntry(".metadata.yml"));
        zos.write("metadata content".getBytes("UTF-8"));
        zos.closeEntry();
        
        zos.finish();
        byte[] zip = baos.toByteArray();
        
        System.out.println("Manual ZIP size: " + zip.length + " bytes");
        
        // Now let's inspect what entries are in the ZIP
        System.out.println("ZIP entries:");
        ZipInputStream zis = new ZipInputStream(new ByteArrayInputStream(zip));
        ZipEntry entry;
        while ((entry = zis.getNextEntry()) != null) {
            System.out.println("  Entry: '" + entry.getName() + "' isDirectory=" + entry.isDirectory());
        }
        zis.close();
        
        // Now try to unzip using ZipUtils
        ZipUtils.UnZipResult result = ZipUtils.unzip(zip);
        System.out.println("MetaDataItem: " + (result.getMetaDataItem() != null ? result.getMetaDataItem().getItemName() : "NULL"));
        System.out.println("ZipItemList size: " + result.getZipItemList().size());
        for (ZipUtils.ZipItem item : result.getZipItemList()) {
            System.out.println("  - " + item.getItemName());
        }
    }
}
EOF

    32	import jakarta.servlet.ServletException;
    33	import org.springframework.beans.factory.annotation.Autowired;
    34	import org.springframework.http.ResponseEntity;
    35	import org.springframework.stereotype.Service;
    36	import org.springframework.web.multipart.MultipartFile;
    37	
    38	import java.io.IOException;
    39	import java.util.List;
    40	import java.util.Map;
    41	
    42	/**
    43	 * Proxy class for handling configuration operations.
    44	 *
    45	 * @author zhangyukun
    46	 */
    47	@Service
    48	public class ConfigProxy {
    49	    
    50	    private final ConfigHandler configHandler;
    51	    
    52	    @Autowired
    53	    public ConfigProxy(ConfigHandler configHandler) {
    54	        this.configHandler = configHandler;
    55	    }
    56	    
    57	    /**
    58	     * Get configure information list.
    59	     */
    60	    public Page<ConfigBasicInfo> getConfigList(int pageNo, int pageSize, String dataId, String group, String namespaceId,
    61	            Map<String, Object> configAdvanceInfo) throws IOException, ServletException, NacosException {
    62	        return configHandler.getConfigList(pageNo, pageSize, dataId, group, namespaceId, configAdvanceInfo);
    63	    }
    64	    
    65	    /**
    66	     * Get the specific configuration information.
    67	     */
    68	    public ConfigDetailInfo getConfigDetail(String dataId, String group, String namespaceId) throws NacosException {
    69	        return configHandler.getConfigDetail(dataId, group, namespaceId);
    70	    }
    71	    
    72	    /**
    73	     * Add or update configuration.
    74	     */
    75	    public Boolean publishConfig(ConfigForm configForm, ConfigRequestInfo configRequestInfo) throws NacosException {
    76	        return configHandler.publishConfig(configForm, configRequestInfo);
    77	    }
    78	    
    79	    /**
    80	     * Delete configuration.
    81	     */
    82	    public Boolean deleteConfig(String dataId, String group, String namespaceId, String tag, String clientIp,
    83	            String srcUser) throws NacosException {
    84	        return configHandler.deleteConfig(dataId, group, namespaceId, tag, clientIp, srcUser);
    85	    }
    86	    
    87	    /**
    88	     * Batch delete configurations.
    89	     */
    90	    public Boolean batchDeleteConfigs(List<Long> ids, String clientIp, String srcUser) throws NacosException {
    91	        return configHandler.batchDeleteConfigs(ids, clientIp, srcUser);
    92	    }
    93	    
    94	    /**
    95	     * Search config list by config detail.
    96	     */
    97	    public Page<ConfigBasicInfo> getConfigListByContent(String search, int pageNo, int pageSize, String dataId, String group,
    98	            String namespaceId, Map<String, Object> configAdvanceInfo) throws NacosException {
    99	        return configHandler.getConfigListByContent(search, pageNo, pageSize, dataId, group, namespaceId,
   100	                configAdvanceInfo);
   101	    }
   102	    
   103	    /**
   104	     * Subscribe to configured client information.
   105	     */
   106	    public ConfigListenerInfo getListeners(String dataId, String group, String namespaceId, boolean aggregation)
   107	            throws Exception {
   108	        return configHandler.getListeners(dataId, group, namespaceId, aggregation);
   109	    }
   110	    
   111	    /**
   112	     * Get subscription information based on IP, tenant, and other parameters.
   113	     */
   114	    public ConfigListenerInfo getAllSubClientConfigByIp(String ip, boolean all, String namespaceId, boolean aggregation)
   115	            throws NacosException {
   116	        return configHandler.getAllSubClientConfigByIp(ip, all, namespaceId, aggregation);
   117	    }
   118	    
   119	    /**
   120	     * New version export config adds metadata.yml file to record config metadata.
   121	     */
   122	    public ResponseEntity<byte[]> exportConfigV2(String dataId, String group, String namespaceId, String appName,
   123	            List<Long> ids) throws Exception {
   124	        return configHandler.exportConfig(dataId, group, namespaceId, appName, ids);
   125	    }
   126	    
   127	    /**
   128	     * Imports and publishes a configuration from a file.
   129	     */
   130	    public Result<Map<String, Object>> importAndPublishConfig(String srcUser, String namespaceId,
   131	            SameConfigPolicy policy, MultipartFile file, String srcIp, String requestIpApp) throws NacosException {
   132	        return configHandler.importAndPublishConfig(srcUser, namespaceId, policy, file, srcIp, requestIpApp);
   133	    }
   134	    
   135	    /**
   136	     * Clone configuration.
   137	     */
   138	    public Result<Map<String, Object>> cloneConfig(String srcUser, String namespaceId,
   139	            List<SameNamespaceCloneConfigBean> configBeansList, SameConfigPolicy policy, String srcIp,
   140	            String requestIpApp) throws NacosException {
   141	        return configHandler.cloneConfig(srcUser, namespaceId, configBeansList, policy, srcIp, requestIpApp);
   142	    }
   143	    
   144	    /**
   145	     * Remove beta configuration based on dataId, group, and namespaceId.
   146	     */
   147	    public boolean removeBetaConfig(String dataId, String group, String namespaceId, String remoteIp,
   148	            String requestIpApp, String srcUser) throws NacosException {
   149	        return configHandler.removeBetaConfig(dataId, group, namespaceId, remoteIp, requestIpApp, srcUser);
   150	    }
   151	    
   152	    /**
   153	     * Query beta configuration based on dataId, group, and namespaceId.
   154	     */
   155	    public ConfigGrayInfo queryBetaConfig(String dataId, String group, String namespaceId)
   156	            throws NacosException {
   157	        return configHandler.queryBetaConfig(dataId, group, namespaceId);
   158	    }
   159	}
