    18	package com.alibaba.nacos.console.handler.config;
    19	
    20	import com.alibaba.nacos.api.config.model.ConfigBasicInfo;
    21	import com.alibaba.nacos.api.config.model.ConfigDetailInfo;
    22	import com.alibaba.nacos.api.config.model.ConfigGrayInfo;
    23	import com.alibaba.nacos.api.config.model.ConfigListenerInfo;
    24	import com.alibaba.nacos.api.config.model.SameConfigPolicy;
    25	import com.alibaba.nacos.api.exception.NacosException;
    26	import com.alibaba.nacos.api.model.Page;
    27	import com.alibaba.nacos.api.model.v2.Result;
    28	import com.alibaba.nacos.config.server.controller.parameters.SameNamespaceCloneConfigBean;
    29	import com.alibaba.nacos.config.server.model.ConfigRequestInfo;
    30	import com.alibaba.nacos.config.server.model.form.ConfigForm;
    31	import jakarta.servlet.ServletException;
    32	import org.springframework.http.ResponseEntity;
    33	import org.springframework.web.multipart.MultipartFile;
    34	
    35	import java.io.IOException;
    36	import java.util.List;
    37	import java.util.Map;
    38	
    39	/**
    40	 * Interface for handling configuration operations.
    41	 *
    42	 * @author zhangyukun
    43	 */
    44	public interface ConfigHandler {
    45	    
    46	    /**
    47	     * Retrieves the configuration based on the specified parameters.
    48	     *
    49	     * @param pageNo            The page number for pagination.
    50	     * @param pageSize          The number of items per page.
    51	     * @param dataId            The identifier of the configuration data.
    52	     * @param group             The group to which the configuration belongs.
    53	     * @param namespaceId       The namespace identifier.
    54	     * @param configAdvanceInfo Additional advanced search criteria.
    55	     * @return ConfigInfo  containing all details of the specified configuration.
    56	     * @throws IOException      If an input or output exception occurs.
    57	     * @throws ServletException If a servlet-specific exception occurs.
    58	     * @throws NacosException   If an error related to Nacos configuration occurs.
    59	     */
    60	    Page<ConfigBasicInfo> getConfigList(int pageNo, int pageSize, String dataId, String group, String namespaceId,
    61	            Map<String, Object> configAdvanceInfo) throws IOException, ServletException, NacosException;
    62	    
    63	    /**
    64	     * Retrieves detailed information about a specific configuration.
    65	     *
    66	     * @param dataId      The identifier of the configuration data.
    67	     * @param group       The group to which the configuration belongs.
    68	     * @param namespaceId The namespace identifier.
    69	     * @return A ConfigAllInfo object containing all details of the specified configuration.
    70	     * @throws NacosException If an error related to Nacos configuration occurs.
    71	     */
    72	    ConfigDetailInfo getConfigDetail(String dataId, String group, String namespaceId) throws NacosException;
    73	    
    74	    /**
    75	     * Publishes a new configuration or updates an existing configuration.
    76	     *
    77	     * @param configForm        The form object containing configuration details.
    78	     * @param configRequestInfo Additional request information related to the configuration.
    79	     * @return A Boolean indicating whether the publish operation was successful.
    80	     * @throws NacosException If an error related to Nacos configuration occurs.
    81	     */
    82	    Boolean publishConfig(ConfigForm configForm, ConfigRequestInfo configRequestInfo) throws NacosException;
    83	    
    84	    /**
    85	     * Deletes a specific configuration.
    86	     *
    87	     * @param dataId      The identifier of the configuration data to delete.
    88	     * @param group       The group to which the configuration belongs.
    89	     * @param namespaceId The namespace identifier.
    90	     * @param tag         The tag associated with the configuration.
    91	     * @param clientIp    The IP address of the client requesting the deletion.
    92	     * @param srcUser     The source user requesting the deletion.
    93	     * @return A Boolean indicating whether the deletion was successful.
    94	     * @throws NacosException If an error related to Nacos configuration occurs.
    95	     */
    96	    Boolean deleteConfig(String dataId, String group, String namespaceId, String tag, String clientIp, String srcUser)
    97	            throws NacosException;
    98	    
    99	    /**
   100	     * Deletes multiple configurations based on their IDs.
   101	     *
   102	     * @param ids      A list of IDs of the configurations to delete.
   103	     * @param clientIp The IP address of the client requesting the deletion.
   104	     * @param srcUser  The source user requesting the deletion.
   105	     * @return A Boolean indicating whether the deletion was successful.
   106	     * @throws NacosException If an error related to Nacos configuration occurs.
   107	     */
   108	    Boolean batchDeleteConfigs(List<Long> ids, String clientIp, String srcUser) throws NacosException;
   109	    
   110	    /**
   111	     * Exports the configuration with metadata based on the specified parameters.
   112	     *
   113	     * @param dataId      The identifier of the configuration data.
   114	     * @param group       The group to which the configuration belongs.
   115	     * @param namespaceId The namespace identifier.
   116	     * @param appName     The application name associated with the configuration.
   117	     * @param ids         A list of IDs of the configurations to export.
   118	     * @return A ResponseEntity containing the exported configuration as a byte array.
   119	     * @throws Exception If an unexpected error occurs during the export process.
   120	     */
   121	    ResponseEntity<byte[]> exportConfig(String dataId, String group, String namespaceId, String appName,
   122	            List<Long> ids) throws Exception;
   123	    
   124	    /**
   125	     * Searches for configurations based on detailed criteria.
   126	     *
   127	     * @param search            The search keyword.
   128	     * @param pageNo            The page number for pagination.
   129	     * @param pageSize          The number of items per page.
   130	     * @param dataId            The identifier of the configuration data.
   131	     * @param group             The group to which the configuration belongs.
   132	     * @param namespaceId       The namespace identifier.
   133	     * @param configAdvanceInfo Additional advanced search criteria.
   134	     * @return A Page object containing a list of ConfigInfo that matches the search criteria.
   135	     * @throws NacosException If an error related to Nacos configuration occurs.
   136	     */
   137	    Page<ConfigBasicInfo> getConfigListByContent(String search, int pageNo, int pageSize, String dataId, String group,
   138	            String namespaceId, Map<String, Object> configAdvanceInfo) throws NacosException;
   139	    
   140	    /**
   141	     * Retrieves the status of listeners for a specific configuration.
   142	     *
   143	     * @param dataId      The identifier of the configuration data.
   144	     * @param group       The group to which the configuration belongs.
   145	     * @param namespaceId The namespace identifier.
   146	     * @param aggregation whether aggregation from other servers
   147	     * @return A ConfigListenerInfo object containing the status of the listeners.
   148	     * @throws Exception If an unexpected error occurs.
   149	     */
   150	    ConfigListenerInfo getListeners(String dataId, String group, String namespaceId, boolean aggregation)
   151	            throws Exception;
   152	    
   153	    /**
   154	     * Get subscription information based on IP, tenant, and other parameters.
   155	     *
   156	     * @param ip IP address of the client
   157	     * @param all Whether to retrieve all configurations
   158	     * @param namespaceId Tenant information
   159	     * @param aggregation whether aggregation from other servers
   160	     * @return ConfigListenerInfo object containing subscription information
   161	     * @throws NacosException If an error occurs while retrieving the subscription information.
   162	     */
   163	    ConfigListenerInfo getAllSubClientConfigByIp(String ip, boolean all, String namespaceId, boolean aggregation)
   164	            throws NacosException;
   165	
   166	    /**
   167	     * Imports and publishes a configuration from a file.
   168	     *
   169	     * @param srcUser      The source user performing the import.
   170	     * @param namespaceId  The namespace identifier.
   171	     * @param policy       The policy for handling existing configurations.
   172	     * @param file         The file containing the configuration to import.
   173	     * @param srcIp        The IP address of the source.
   174	     * @param requestIpApp The IP address of the requester.
   175	     * @return A Result object containing the status and additional information about the operation.
   176	     * @throws NacosException If an error related to Nacos configuration occurs.
   177	     */
   178	    Result<Map<String, Object>> importAndPublishConfig(String srcUser, String namespaceId, SameConfigPolicy policy,
   179	            MultipartFile file, String srcIp, String requestIpApp) throws NacosException;
   180	    
   181	    
   182	    /**
   183	     * Clones an existing configuration to a different namespace.
   184	     *
   185	     * @param srcUser         The source user performing the clone operation.
   186	     * @param namespaceId     The namespace identifier where the configuration will be cloned to.
   187	     * @param configBeansList A list of configurations to be cloned.
   188	     * @param policy          The policy for handling existing configurations in the target namespace.
   189	     * @param srcIp           The IP address of the source.
   190	     * @param requestIpApp    The IP address of the requester.
   191	     * @return A Result object containing the status and additional information about the operation.
   192	     * @throws NacosException If an error related to Nacos configuration occurs.
   193	     */
   194	    Result<Map<String, Object>> cloneConfig(String srcUser, String namespaceId,
   195	            List<SameNamespaceCloneConfigBean> configBeansList, SameConfigPolicy policy, String srcIp,
   196	            String requestIpApp) throws NacosException;
   197	    
   198	    /**
   199	     * Remove beta configuration based on dataId, group, and namespaceId.
   200	     *
   201	     * @param dataId       the dataId
   202	     * @param group        the group
   203	     * @param namespaceId  the namespaceId
   204	     * @param remoteIp     the IP address of the client making the request
   205	     * @param requestIpApp the name of the application making the request
   206	     * @param srcUser      the src user performing the operation
   207	     * @return true if the beta configuration is successfully removed
   208	     * @throws NacosException if an error occurs while removing the beta configuration
   209	     */
   210	    boolean removeBetaConfig(String dataId, String group, String namespaceId, String remoteIp, String requestIpApp,
   211	            String srcUser) throws NacosException;
   212	    
   213	    /**
   214	     * Query beta configuration based on dataId, group, and namespaceId.
   215	     *
   216	     * @param dataId      the dataId
   217	     * @param group       the group
   218	     * @param namespaceId the namespaceId
   219	     * @return ConfigInfo4Beta containing the beta configuration details
   220	     * @throws NacosException if an error occurs while querying the beta configuration
   221	     */
   222	    ConfigGrayInfo queryBetaConfig(String dataId, String group, String namespaceId) throws NacosException;
   223	}

    92	@Service
    93	@EnabledInnerHandler
    94	@Conditional(ConditionFunctionEnabled.ConditionConfigEnabled.class)
    95	public class ConfigInnerHandler implements ConfigHandler {

   123	     */
   124	    private boolean oldTableVersion;

   126	    public ConfigInnerHandler(ConfigOperationService configOperationService,
   127	            ConfigInfoPersistService configInfoPersistService, ConfigDetailService configDetailService,
   128	            NamespacePersistService namespacePersistService, ConfigInfoBetaPersistService configInfoBetaPersistService,
   129	            ConfigInfoGrayPersistService configInfoGrayPersistService,
   130	            ConfigListenerStateDelegate configListenerStateDelegate, ConfigMigrateService configMigrateService) {
   131	        this.configOperationService = configOperationService;
   132	        this.configInfoPersistService = configInfoPersistService;
   133	        this.configDetailService = configDetailService;
   134	        this.namespacePersistService = namespacePersistService;
   135	        this.configInfoBetaPersistService = configInfoBetaPersistService;
   136	        this.configInfoGrayPersistService = configInfoGrayPersistService;
   137	        this.configListenerStateDelegate = configListenerStateDelegate;
   138	        this.configMigrateService = configMigrateService;
   139	        this.oldTableVersion = namespacePersistService.isExistTable("config_info_beta");
   140	    }

   142	    @Override
   143	    public Page<ConfigBasicInfo> getConfigList(int pageNo, int pageSize, String dataId, String group,
   144	            String namespaceId, Map<String, Object> configAdvanceInfo)
   145	            throws IOException, ServletException, NacosException {
   146	        Page<ConfigInfo> result = configInfoPersistService.findConfigInfoLike4Page(pageNo, pageSize, dataId, group,
   147	                namespaceId, configAdvanceInfo);
   148	        return transferToConfigBasicInfo(result);
   149	    }
   150	    
   151	    @Override
   152	    public ConfigDetailInfo getConfigDetail(String dataId, String group, String namespaceId) throws NacosException {
   153	        ConfigAllInfo configAllInfo = configInfoPersistService.findConfigAllInfo(dataId, group, namespaceId);
   154	        if (null == configAllInfo) {
   155	            return null;
   156	        }
   157	        return ResponseUtil.transferToConfigDetailInfo(configAllInfo);
   158	    }
   159	    
   160	    @Override
   161	    public Boolean publishConfig(ConfigForm configForm, ConfigRequestInfo configRequestInfo) throws NacosException {
   162	        String encryptedDataKeyFinal = configForm.getEncryptedDataKey();
   163	        if (StringUtils.isBlank(encryptedDataKeyFinal)) {
   164	            // encrypted
   165	            Pair<String, String> pair = EncryptionHandler.encryptHandler(configForm.getDataId(),
   166	                    configForm.getContent());
   167	            configForm.setContent(pair.getSecond());
   168	            encryptedDataKeyFinal = pair.getFirst();
   169	        }
   170	        return configOperationService.publishConfig(configForm, configRequestInfo, encryptedDataKeyFinal);
   171	    }
   172	    
   173	    @Override
   174	    public Boolean deleteConfig(String dataId, String group, String namespaceId, String tag, String clientIp,
   175	            String srcUser) throws NacosException {
   176	        return configOperationService.deleteConfig(dataId, group, namespaceId, tag, clientIp, srcUser, Constants.HTTP);
   177	    }
   178	    
   179	    @Override
   180	    public Boolean batchDeleteConfigs(List<Long> ids, String clientIp, String srcUser) {
   181	        for (Long id : ids) {
   182	            ConfigInfo configInfo = configInfoPersistService.findConfigInfo(id);
   183	            if (configInfo == null) {
   184	                LOGGER.warn("[deleteConfigs] configInfo is null, id: {}", id);
   185	                continue;
   186	            }
   187	            configOperationService.deleteConfig(configInfo.getDataId(), configInfo.getGroup(), configInfo.getTenant(),
   188	                    null, clientIp, srcUser, Constants.HTTP);
   189	        }
   190	        return true;
   191	    }
   192	    
   193	    @Override
   194	    public Page<ConfigBasicInfo> getConfigListByContent(String search, int pageNo, int pageSize, String dataId,
   195	            String group, String namespaceId, Map<String, Object> configAdvanceInfo) throws NacosException {
   196	        try {
   197	            Page<ConfigInfo> result = configDetailService.findConfigInfoPage(search, pageNo, pageSize, dataId, group,
   198	                    namespaceId, configAdvanceInfo);
   199	            return transferToConfigBasicInfo(result);
   200	        } catch (Exception e) {
   201	            String errorMsg = "serialize page error, dataId=" + dataId + ", group=" + group;
   202	            LOGGER.error(errorMsg, e);
   203	            throw e;
   204	        }
   205	    }

   207	    @Override
   208	    public ConfigListenerInfo getListeners(String dataId, String group, String namespaceId, boolean aggregation)
   209	            throws Exception {
   210	        return configListenerStateDelegate.getListenerState(dataId, group, namespaceId, aggregation);
   211	    }
   212	    
   213	    @Override
   214	    public ConfigListenerInfo getAllSubClientConfigByIp(String ip, boolean all, String namespaceId,
   215	            boolean aggregation) {
   216	        ConfigListenerInfo result = configListenerStateDelegate.getListenerStateByIp(ip, aggregation);
   217	        result.setQueryType(ConfigListenerInfo.QUERY_TYPE_IP);
   218	        Map<String, String> configMd5Status = new HashMap<>(100);
   219	        if (result.getListenersStatus() == null || result.getListenersStatus().isEmpty()) {
   220	            return result;
   221	        }
   222	        Map<String, String> status = result.getListenersStatus();
   223	        for (Map.Entry<String, String> config : status.entrySet()) {
   224	            if (!StringUtils.isBlank(namespaceId) && config.getKey().contains(namespaceId)) {
   225	                configMd5Status.put(config.getKey(), config.getValue());
   226	                continue;
   227	            }
   228	            if (all) {
   229	                configMd5Status.put(config.getKey(), config.getValue());
   230	            } else {
   231	                String[] configKeys = GroupKey2.parseKey(config.getKey());
   232	                if (StringUtils.isBlank(configKeys[2])) {
   233	                    configMd5Status.put(config.getKey(), config.getValue());
   234	                }
   235	            }
   236	        }
   237	        result.setListenersStatus(configMd5Status);
   238	        return result;
   239	    }
   240	    
   241	    @Override
   242	    public ResponseEntity<byte[]> exportConfig(String dataId, String group, String namespaceId, String appName,
   243	            List<Long> ids) throws Exception {
   244	        List<ConfigAllInfo> dataList = configInfoPersistService.findAllConfigInfo4Export(dataId, group, namespaceId,
   245	                appName, ids);
   246	        List<ZipUtils.ZipItem> zipItemList = new ArrayList<>();
   247	        List<ConfigMetadata.ConfigExportItem> configMetadataItems = new ArrayList<>();
   248	        for (ConfigAllInfo ci : dataList) {
   249	            ConfigMetadata.ConfigExportItem configMetadataItem = new ConfigMetadata.ConfigExportItem();
   250	            configMetadataItem.setAppName(ci.getAppName());
   251	            configMetadataItem.setDataId(ci.getDataId());
   252	            configMetadataItem.setDesc(ci.getDesc());
   253	            configMetadataItem.setGroup(ci.getGroup());
   254	            configMetadataItem.setType(ci.getType());
   255	            configMetadataItems.add(configMetadataItem);
   256	            Pair<String, String> pair = EncryptionHandler.decryptHandler(ci.getDataId(), ci.getEncryptedDataKey(),
   257	                    ci.getContent());
   258	            String itemName = ci.getGroup() + Constants.CONFIG_EXPORT_ITEM_FILE_SEPARATOR + ci.getDataId();
   259	            zipItemList.add(new ZipUtils.ZipItem(itemName, pair.getSecond()));
   260	        }
   261	        ConfigMetadata configMetadata = new ConfigMetadata();
   262	        configMetadata.setMetadata(configMetadataItems);
   263	        zipItemList.add(
   264	                new ZipUtils.ZipItem(Constants.CONFIG_EXPORT_METADATA_NEW, YamlParserUtil.dumpObject(configMetadata)));
   265	        HttpHeaders headers = new HttpHeaders();
   266	        String fileName =
   267	                EXPORT_CONFIG_FILE_NAME + DateFormatUtils.format(new Date(), EXPORT_CONFIG_FILE_NAME_DATE_FORMAT)
   268	                        + EXPORT_CONFIG_FILE_NAME_EXT;
   269	        headers.add("Content-Disposition", "attachment;filename=" + fileName);
   270	        return new ResponseEntity<>(ZipUtils.zip(zipItemList), headers, HttpStatus.OK);
   271	    }
   272	    
   273	    @Override
   274	    public Result<Map<String, Object>> importAndPublishConfig(String srcUser, String namespaceId,
   275	            SameConfigPolicy policy, MultipartFile file, String srcIp, String requestIpApp) throws NacosException {
   276	        Map<String, Object> failedData = new HashMap<>(4);
   277	        if (Objects.isNull(file)) {
   278	            return Result.failure(ErrorCode.DATA_EMPTY, failedData);
   279	        }
   280	        if (StringUtils.isNotBlank(namespaceId) && !NamespaceUtil.isDefaultNamespaceId(namespaceId)
   281	                && namespacePersistService.tenantInfoCountByTenantId(namespaceId) <= 0) {
   282	            failedData.put("succCount", 0);
   283	            return Result.failure(ErrorCode.NAMESPACE_NOT_EXIST, failedData);
   284	        }
   285	        
   286	        List<ConfigAllInfo> configInfoList = new ArrayList<>();
   287	        List<Map<String, String>> unrecognizedList = new ArrayList<>();
   288	        try {
   289	            ZipUtils.UnZipResult unziped = ZipUtils.unzip(file.getBytes());
   290	            Result<Map<String, Object>> errorResult;
   291	            errorResult = parseImportDataV2(srcUser, unziped, configInfoList, unrecognizedList, namespaceId);
   292	            if (errorResult != null) {
   293	                return errorResult;
   294	            }
   295	        } catch (IOException e) {
   296	            failedData.put("succCount", 0);
   297	            LOGGER.error("parsing data failed", e);
   298	            return Result.failure(ErrorCode.PARSING_DATA_FAILED, failedData);
   299	        }
   300	        
   301	        if (CollectionUtils.isEmpty(configInfoList)) {
   302	            failedData.put("succCount", 0);
   303	            return Result.failure(ErrorCode.DATA_EMPTY, failedData);
   304	        }
   305	        final Timestamp time = TimeUtils.getCurrentTime();
   306	        Map<String, Object> saveResult = configInfoPersistService.batchInsertOrUpdate(configInfoList, srcUser, srcIp,
   307	                null, policy);
   308	        for (ConfigInfo configInfo : configInfoList) {
   309	            ConfigChangePublisher.notifyConfigChange(
   310	                    new ConfigDataChangeEvent(configInfo.getDataId(), configInfo.getGroup(), configInfo.getTenant(),
   311	                            time.getTime()));
   312	            ConfigTraceService.logPersistenceEvent(configInfo.getDataId(), configInfo.getGroup(),
   313	                    configInfo.getTenant(), requestIpApp, time.getTime(), InetUtils.getSelfIP(),
   314	                    ConfigTraceService.PERSISTENCE_EVENT, ConfigTraceService.PERSISTENCE_TYPE_PUB,
   315	                    configInfo.getContent());
   316	        }
   317	        // unrecognizedCount
   318	        if (!unrecognizedList.isEmpty()) {
   319	            saveResult.put("unrecognizedCount", unrecognizedList.size());
   320	            saveResult.put("unrecognizedData", unrecognizedList);
   321	        }
   322	        return Result.success(saveResult);
   323	    }
   324	    
   325	    /**
   326	     * new version import config add .metadata.yml file.
   327	     *
   328	     * @param unziped          export file.
   329	     * @param configInfoList   parse file result.
   330	     * @param unrecognizedList unrecognized file.
   331	     * @param namespace        import namespace.
   332	     * @return error result.
   333	     */
   334	    private Result<Map<String, Object>> parseImportDataV2(String srcUser, ZipUtils.UnZipResult unziped,
   335	            List<ConfigAllInfo> configInfoList, List<Map<String, String>> unrecognizedList, String namespace) {
   336	        ZipUtils.ZipItem metaDataItem = unziped.getMetaDataItem();
   337	        String metaData = metaDataItem.getItemData();
   338	        Map<String, Object> failedData = new HashMap<>(4);
   339	        
   340	        ConfigMetadata configMetadata = YamlParserUtil.loadObject(metaData, ConfigMetadata.class);
   341	        if (configMetadata == null || CollectionUtils.isEmpty(configMetadata.getMetadata())) {
   342	            failedData.put("succCount", 0);
   343	            return Result.failure(ErrorCode.METADATA_ILLEGAL, failedData);
   344	        }
   345	        List<ConfigMetadata.ConfigExportItem> configExportItems = configMetadata.getMetadata();
   346	        // check config metadata
   347	        for (ConfigMetadata.ConfigExportItem configExportItem : configExportItems) {
   348	            if (StringUtils.isBlank(configExportItem.getDataId()) || StringUtils.isBlank(configExportItem.getGroup())
   349	                    || StringUtils.isBlank(configExportItem.getType())) {
   350	                failedData.put("succCount", 0);
   351	                return Result.failure(ErrorCode.METADATA_ILLEGAL, failedData);
   352	            }
   353	        }
   354	        
   355	        List<ZipUtils.ZipItem> zipItemList = unziped.getZipItemList();
   356	        Set<String> metaDataKeys = configExportItems.stream()
   357	                .map(metaItem -> GroupKey.getKey(metaItem.getDataId(), metaItem.getGroup()))
   358	                .collect(Collectors.toSet());
   359	        
   360	        Map<String, String> configContentMap = new HashMap<>(zipItemList.size());
   361	        int itemNameLength = 2;
   362	        zipItemList.forEach(item -> {
   363	            String itemName = item.getItemName();
   364	            String[] groupAdnDataId = itemName.split(Constants.CONFIG_EXPORT_ITEM_FILE_SEPARATOR);
   365	            if (groupAdnDataId.length != itemNameLength) {
   366	                Map<String, String> unrecognizedItem = new HashMap<>(2);
   367	                unrecognizedItem.put("itemName", item.getItemName());
   368	                unrecognizedList.add(unrecognizedItem);
   369	                return;
   370	            }
   371	            
   372	            String group = groupAdnDataId[0];
   373	            String dataId = groupAdnDataId[1];
   374	            String key = GroupKey.getKey(dataId, group);
   375	            // metadata does not contain config file
   376	            if (!metaDataKeys.contains(key)) {
   377	                Map<String, String> unrecognizedItem = new HashMap<>(2);
   378	                unrecognizedItem.put("itemName", "未在元数据中找到: " + item.getItemName());
   379	                unrecognizedList.add(unrecognizedItem);
   380	                return;
   381	            }
   382	            String itemData = item.getItemData();
   383	            configContentMap.put(key, itemData);
   384	        });
   385	        
   386	        for (ConfigMetadata.ConfigExportItem configExportItem : configExportItems) {
   387	            String dataId = configExportItem.getDataId();
   388	            String group = configExportItem.getGroup();
   389	            String content = configContentMap.get(GroupKey.getKey(dataId, group));
   390	            // config file not in metadata
   391	            if (content == null) {
   392	                Map<String, String> unrecognizedItem = new HashMap<>(2);
   393	                unrecognizedItem.put("itemName", "未在文件中找到: " + group + "/" + dataId);
   394	                unrecognizedList.add(unrecognizedItem);
   395	                continue;
   396	            }
   397	            // encrypted
   398	            Pair<String, String> pair = EncryptionHandler.encryptHandler(dataId, content);
   399	            content = pair.getSecond();
   400	            
   401	            ConfigAllInfo ci = new ConfigAllInfo();
   402	            ci.setGroup(group);
   403	            ci.setDataId(dataId);
   404	            ci.setContent(content);
   405	            ci.setType(configExportItem.getType());
   406	            ci.setDesc(configExportItem.getDesc());
   407	            ci.setAppName(configExportItem.getAppName());
   408	            ci.setTenant(namespace);
   409	            ci.setEncryptedDataKey(pair.getFirst());
   410	            ci.setCreateUser(srcUser);
   411	            configInfoList.add(ci);
   412	        }
   413	        return null;
   414	    }
   415	    
   416	    @Override
   417	    public Result<Map<String, Object>> cloneConfig(String srcUser, String namespaceId,
   418	            List<SameNamespaceCloneConfigBean> configBeansList, SameConfigPolicy policy, String srcIp,
   419	            String requestIpApp) throws NacosException {
   420	        Map<String, Object> failedData = new HashMap<>(4);
   421	        if (CollectionUtils.isEmpty(configBeansList)) {
   422	            failedData.put("succCount", 0);
   423	            return Result.failure(ErrorCode.NO_SELECTED_CONFIG, failedData);
   424	        }
   425	        if (StringUtils.isNotBlank(namespaceId) && !NamespaceUtil.isDefaultNamespaceId(namespaceId)
   426	                && namespacePersistService.tenantInfoCountByTenantId(namespaceId) <= 0) {
   427	            failedData.put("succCount", 0);
   428	            return Result.failure(ErrorCode.NAMESPACE_NOT_EXIST, failedData);
   429	        }
   430	        
   431	        List<Long> idList = new ArrayList<>(configBeansList.size());
   432	        Map<Long, SameNamespaceCloneConfigBean> configBeansMap = configBeansList.stream()
   433	                .collect(Collectors.toMap(SameNamespaceCloneConfigBean::getCfgId, cfg -> {
   434	                    idList.add(cfg.getCfgId());
   435	                    return cfg;
   436	                }, (k1, k2) -> k1));
   437	        
   438	        List<ConfigAllInfo> queryedDataList = configInfoPersistService.findAllConfigInfo4Export(null, null, null, null,
   439	                idList);
   440	        
   441	        if (queryedDataList == null || queryedDataList.isEmpty()) {
   442	            failedData.put("succCount", 0);
   443	            return Result.failure(ErrorCode.DATA_EMPTY, failedData);
   444	        }
   445	        
   446	        List<ConfigAllInfo> configInfoList4Clone = new ArrayList<>(queryedDataList.size());
   447	        
   448	        for (ConfigAllInfo ci : queryedDataList) {
   449	            SameNamespaceCloneConfigBean paramBean = configBeansMap.get(ci.getId());
   450	            ConfigAllInfo ci4save = new ConfigAllInfo();
   451	            ci4save.setTenant(namespaceId);
   452	            ci4save.setType(ci.getType());
   453	            ci4save.setGroup((paramBean != null && StringUtils.isNotBlank(paramBean.getGroup())) ? paramBean.getGroup()
   454	                    : ci.getGroup());
   455	            ci4save.setDataId(
   456	                    (paramBean != null && StringUtils.isNotBlank(paramBean.getDataId())) ? paramBean.getDataId()
   457	                            : ci.getDataId());
   458	            ci4save.setContent(ci.getContent());
   459	            if (StringUtils.isNotBlank(ci.getAppName())) {
   460	                ci4save.setAppName(ci.getAppName());
   461	            }
   462	            ci4save.setDesc(ci.getDesc());
   463	            ci4save.setEncryptedDataKey(
   464	                    ci.getEncryptedDataKey() == null ? StringUtils.EMPTY : ci.getEncryptedDataKey());
   465	            configInfoList4Clone.add(ci4save);
   466	        }
   467	        
   468	        final Timestamp time = TimeUtils.getCurrentTime();
   469	        Map<String, Object> saveResult = configInfoPersistService.batchInsertOrUpdate(configInfoList4Clone, srcUser,
   470	                srcIp, null, policy);
   471	        for (ConfigInfo configInfo : configInfoList4Clone) {
   472	            ConfigChangePublisher.notifyConfigChange(
   473	                    new ConfigDataChangeEvent(configInfo.getDataId(), configInfo.getGroup(), configInfo.getTenant(),
   474	                            time.getTime()));
   475	            ConfigTraceService.logPersistenceEvent(configInfo.getDataId(), configInfo.getGroup(),
   476	                    configInfo.getTenant(), requestIpApp, time.getTime(), InetUtils.getSelfIP(),
   477	                    ConfigTraceService.PERSISTENCE_EVENT, ConfigTraceService.PERSISTENCE_TYPE_PUB,
   478	                    configInfo.getContent());
   479	        }
   480	        return Result.success(saveResult);
   481	    }
   482	    
   483	    @Override
   484	    public boolean removeBetaConfig(String dataId, String group, String namespaceId, String remoteIp,
   485	            String requestIpApp, String srcUser) {
   486	        try {
   487	            configInfoGrayPersistService.removeConfigInfoGray(dataId, group, namespaceId, BetaGrayRule.TYPE_BETA,
   488	                    remoteIp, srcUser);
   489	            configMigrateService.removeConfigInfoGrayMigrate(dataId, group, namespaceId, BetaGrayRule.TYPE_BETA,
   490	                    remoteIp, srcUser);
   491	        } catch (Throwable e) {
   492	            LOGGER.error("remove beta data error", e);
   493	            return false;
   494	        }
   495	        ConfigTraceService.logPersistenceEvent(dataId, group, namespaceId, requestIpApp, System.currentTimeMillis(),
   496	                remoteIp, ConfigTraceService.PERSISTENCE_EVENT_BETA, ConfigTraceService.PERSISTENCE_TYPE_REMOVE, null);
   497	        if (PropertyUtil.isGrayCompatibleModel() && oldTableVersion) {
   498	            configInfoBetaPersistService.removeConfigInfo4Beta(dataId, group, namespaceId);
   499	        }
   500	        ConfigChangePublisher.notifyConfigChange(
   501	                new ConfigDataChangeEvent(dataId, group, namespaceId, BetaGrayRule.TYPE_BETA,
   502	                        System.currentTimeMillis()));
   503	        return true;
   504	        
   505	    }
   506	    
   507	    @Override
   508	    public ConfigGrayInfo queryBetaConfig(String dataId, String group, String namespaceId) throws NacosException {
   509	        ConfigInfoGrayWrapper beta4Gray = configInfoGrayPersistService.findConfigInfo4Gray(dataId, group, namespaceId,
   510	                "beta");
   511	        if (Objects.nonNull(beta4Gray)) {
   512	            String encryptedDataKey = beta4Gray.getEncryptedDataKey();
   513	            Pair<String, String> pair = EncryptionHandler.decryptHandler(dataId, encryptedDataKey,
   514	                    beta4Gray.getContent());
   515	            beta4Gray.setContent(pair.getSecond());
   516	
   517	            //find the corresponding production config to get the `type` field, because the `type` field is not stored in the beta table
   518	            ConfigInfoWrapper productionConfig = configInfoPersistService.findConfigInfo(dataId, group, namespaceId);
   519	            if (Objects.nonNull(productionConfig)) {
   520	                beta4Gray.setType(productionConfig.getType());
   521	            }
   522	            return ResponseUtil.transferToConfigGrayInfo(beta4Gray);
   523	        }
   524	        return null;
   525	    }
   526	    
   527	    private Page<ConfigBasicInfo> transferToConfigBasicInfo(Page<ConfigInfo> configInfoPage) {
   528	        Page<ConfigBasicInfo> result = new Page<>();
   529	        result.setTotalCount(configInfoPage.getTotalCount());
   530	        result.setPagesAvailable(configInfoPage.getPagesAvailable());
   531	        result.setPageNumber(configInfoPage.getPageNumber());
   532	        result.setPageItems(configInfoPage.getPageItems().stream().map(ResponseUtil::transferToConfigBasicInfo)
   533	                .collect(Collectors.toList()));
   534	        return result;
   535	    }
   536	    
   537	}

import com.alibaba.nacos.config.server.constant.Constants;

public class ReproduceZipTest3 {
    public static void main(String[] args) throws Exception {
        // Test the exact scenario from the PR: 
        // A ZIP with DEFAULT_GROUP/application.yml and meta_data (text format)
        System.out.println("=== Test: PR Scenario Case 1 (simple meta_data text file) ===");

        testCase2();
        
        System.out.println("\n=== Test: ZIP without any metadata (simulating broken export) ===");
        testCase3();
    }
    
    static void testCase1() {
        // This is the old format from PR description: meta_data file with "DEFAULT_GROUP|application.yml|"
        List<ZipUtils.ZipItem> items = new ArrayList<>();
        items.add(new ZipUtils.ZipItem("DEFAULT_GROUP/application.yml", "some: content"));
        items.add(new ZipUtils.ZipItem("meta_data", "DEFAULT_GROUP|application.yml|"));
        
        byte[] zip = ZipUtils.zip(items);
        ZipUtils.UnZipResult result = ZipUtils.unzip(zip);
        
        System.out.println("MetaDataItem: " + (result.getMetaDataItem() != null ? result.getMetaDataItem().getItemName() : "NULL"));
        System.out.println("ZipItemList size: " + result.getZipItemList().size());
        
        // The old format uses "meta_data" but the code looks for ".meta.yml" or ".metadata.yml"
        // So metaDataItem will be null!
        if (result.getMetaDataItem() == null) {
            System.out.println("BUG REPRODUCED: metaDataItem is null when using 'meta_data' filename!");
        }
    }
    
    static void testCase2() {
        // This is what the current export produces

        items.add(new ZipUtils.ZipItem(".metadata.yml", "metadata: [...]"));
        
        byte[] zip = ZipUtils.zip(items);
        ZipUtils.UnZipResult result = ZipUtils.unzip(zip);

        System.out.println("ZipItemList size: " + result.getZipItemList().size());
    }

        // ZIP without any metadata

        items.add(new ZipUtils.ZipItem("DEFAULT_GROUP/application.yml", "some: content"));

        ZipUtils.UnZipResult result = ZipUtils.unzip(zip);
        
        System.out.println("MetaDataItem: " + (result.getMetaDataItem() != null ? result.getMetaDataItem().getItemName() : "NULL"));

        if (result.getMetaDataItem() == null) {
            System.out.println("BUG REPRODUCED: metaDataItem is null when no metadata file exists!");
        }
    }
}

Now let me think about the fixes needed:

**Fix 1: Support the `meta_data` filename in `ZipUtils.unzip`**
The PR description says the simple format is `GROUP|dataId|tenantId`. But looking at the code, the old format uses `meta_data` filename with pipe-separated values. The new format uses `.metadata.yml` with YAML. We should support both.

Actually, looking at this more carefully, the PR description says the export doesn't include `meta_data`. But the current code exports `.metadata.yml`. The issue is that:

1. The `ZipUtils.unzip` doesn't recognize `meta_data` as a metadata file (only `.meta.yml` and `.metadata.yml`)
2. When no metadata is found, the import code throws NPE

Let me look at what changes are needed:

1. In `ZipUtils.unzip`: Add support for `meta_data` filename
2. In `ConfigControllerV3.parseImportDataV2` and `ConfigInnerHandler.parseImportDataV2`: Handle the case when `metaDataItem` is null

But actually, thinking about this more: the PR description mentions that the old format uses `meta_data` with pipe-separated values. The new format uses YAML. The code currently only handles the YAML format. 

But the PR also says that even with a properly formatted ZIP (exported from the console), the import fails. That's weird because my test shows the export/import cycle works with `.metadata.yml`.

   222	        
   223	        Page<ConfigInfo> page = new Page<>();
   224	        page.setTotalCount(15);
   225	        page.setPageNumber(1);
   226	        page.setPagesAvailable(2);
   227	        page.setPageItems(configInfoList);

   232	        
   233	        MockHttpServletRequestBuilder builder = MockMvcRequestBuilders.get(Constants.CONFIG_ADMIN_V3_PATH + "/list")
   234	                .param("search", "accurate").param("dataId", "test").param("groupName", "test").param("appName", "")
   235	                .param("namespaceId", "").param("config_tags", "").param("pageNo", "1").param("pageSize", "10")
   236	                .param("config_detail", "");
   237	        String actualValue = mockmvc.perform(builder).andReturn().getResponse().getContentAsString();
   238	        String data = JacksonUtils.toObj(actualValue).get("data").toString();

   351	    @Test
   352	    void testImportAndPublishConfigV2() throws Exception {
   353	        List<ZipUtils.ZipItem> zipItems = new ArrayList<>();
   354	        String dataId = "dataId23456.json";
   355	        String groupName = "group132";
   356	        String content = "content1234";
   357	        ZipUtils.ZipItem zipItem = new ZipUtils.ZipItem(groupName + "/" + dataId, content);
   358	        zipItems.add(zipItem);
   359	        ConfigMetadata configMetadata = new ConfigMetadata();
   360	        configMetadata.setMetadata(new ArrayList<>());
   361	        ConfigMetadata.ConfigExportItem configExportItem = new ConfigMetadata.ConfigExportItem();
   362	        configExportItem.setDataId(dataId);
   363	        configExportItem.setGroup(groupName);
   364	        configExportItem.setType("json");
   365	        configExportItem.setAppName("appna123");
   366	        configMetadata.getMetadata().add(configExportItem);
   367	        ZipUtils.UnZipResult unziped = new ZipUtils.UnZipResult(zipItems,
   368	                new ZipUtils.ZipItem(Constants.CONFIG_EXPORT_METADATA_NEW, YamlParserUtil.dumpObject(configMetadata)));
   369	        MockMultipartFile file = new MockMultipartFile("file", "test.zip", "application/zip", "test".getBytes());
   370	        try (MockedStatic<ZipUtils> zipUtilsMockedStatic = Mockito.mockStatic(ZipUtils.class)) {
   371	            zipUtilsMockedStatic.when(() -> ZipUtils.unzip(eq(file.getBytes()))).thenReturn(unziped);
   372	            when(namespacePersistService.tenantInfoCountByTenantId("public")).thenReturn(1);
   373	            Map<String, Object> map = new HashMap<>();
   374	            map.put("test", "test");
   375	            when(configInfoPersistService.batchInsertOrUpdate(anyList(), anyString(), anyString(), any(),
   376	                    any())).thenReturn(map);
   377	            
   378	            MockHttpServletRequestBuilder builder = MockMvcRequestBuilders.multipart(
   379	                            Constants.CONFIG_ADMIN_V3_PATH + "/import").file(file).param("src_user", "test")
   380	                    .param("namespace", "public").param("policy", "ABORT");
   381	            
   382	            String actualValue = mockmvc.perform(builder).andReturn().getResponse().getContentAsString();
   383	            
   384	            String code = JacksonUtils.toObj(actualValue).get("code").toString();
   385	            assertEquals("0", code);
   386	            Map<String, Object> resultMap = JacksonUtils.toObj(JacksonUtils.toObj(actualValue).get("data").toString(),
   387	                    Map.class);
   388	            assertEquals(map.get("test"), resultMap.get("test").toString());
   389	        }
   390	    }

Now I understand the full picture. Let me now plan the fixes:

**The bugs:**

1. **`ZipUtils.unzip` doesn't recognize `meta_data` as a metadata file**: It only looks for `.meta.yml` and `.metadata.yml`. The PR description mentions a `meta_data` file (no dot prefix, different format). We need to also support `meta_data` as a metadata filename.

2. **`parseImportDataV2` in both `ConfigControllerV3` and `ConfigInnerHandler` throws NPE when `metaDataItem` is null**: If the ZIP has no metadata file, `metaDataItem` is null and calling `getItemData()` on it throws NPE. We should return a proper error response instead.

3. **The export function in `ConfigControllerV3` and `ConfigInnerHandler` does include `.metadata.yml`** - so the export actually seems correct for the new format. But maybe there's a need to also support the old `meta_data` format?

Wait, let me re-read the PR description more carefully:

> 1. **Export Bug**: When exporting configurations, the generated ZIP file does NOT include the `meta_data` file that is required for import. The exported ZIP only contains the configuration files in group directories.

So the PR says the export doesn't include `meta_data`. But looking at the code, the export includes `.metadata.yml` (YAML format), not `meta_data` (pipe-separated format). Maybe the frontend is expecting `meta_data` and that's why it fails?

Actually wait - looking at the PR description again, it says the expected ZIP has `meta_data` (without dot prefix). But the code adds `.metadata.yml`. Maybe the console frontend or some older client expects `meta_data`?

But regardless, the key issue is:

1. The `ZipUtils.unzip` should also recognize `meta_data` as a metadata file
2. The import functions should handle null `metaDataItem` gracefully

Let me also check if there are any other places that need to handle the old `meta_data` format. Let me look at how `meta_data` is parsed vs `.metadata.yml`:

- `.metadata.yml` is YAML format: `YamlParserUtil.loadObject(metaData, ConfigMetadata.class)`
- `meta_data` is pipe-separated format: `GROUP|dataId|tenantId`

The PR says `meta_data` contains:
```
DEFAULT_GROUP|application.yml|
```

But the current import code (`parseImportDataV2`) only handles the YAML format. To support the old format, we would need to parse the pipe-separated format too.

However, the minimal fix that the PR seems to request is:
1. Make `ZipUtils.unzip` recognize `meta_data` as metadata
2. Handle null `metaDataItem` gracefully

But actually, even if we recognize `meta_data`, the `parseImportDataV2` method would still fail because it expects YAML format, not pipe-separated. So we'd need to handle both formats there too.

1. In `ZipUtils.unzip`: Add support for `meta_data` filename (in addition to `.meta.yml` and `.metadata.yml`)
2. In `ConfigControllerV3.parseImportDataV2` and `ConfigInnerHandler.parseImportDataV2`: Handle null `metaDataItem` by returning an error. Also, support parsing the old pipe-separated format.

But actually, looking at this more, the PR description says:
> 2. **Import Bug**: The import function expects a `meta_data` file in the ZIP, but even when providing a correctly formatted `meta_data` file, the import still fails.

So users are providing a `meta_data` file (pipe-separated format) and it fails. The reason is:
1. `ZipUtils.unzip` doesn't recognize `meta_data` as metadata (only `.meta.yml` and `.metadata.yml`)
2. Even if it did, `parseImportDataV2` would try to parse it as YAML, which would fail

So the fix should:
1. Add `meta_data` to the recognized metadata filenames in `ZipUtils.unzip`
2. In `parseImportDataV2`, detect whether the metadata is YAML or pipe-separated, and parse accordingly

    52	        }
    53	        
    54	        public String getItemName() {
    55	            return itemName;
    56	        }
    57	        
    58	        public void setItemName(String itemName) {
    59	            this.itemName = itemName;
    60	        }
    61	        
    62	        public String getItemData() {
    63	            return itemData;
    64	        }
    65	        
    66	        public void setItemData(String itemData) {
    67	            this.itemData = itemData;
    68	        }
    69	    }
    70	    
    71	    public static class UnZipResult {
    72	        
    73	        private List<ZipItem> zipItemList;
    74	        
    75	        private ZipItem metaDataItem;
    76	        
    77	        public UnZipResult(List<ZipItem> zipItemList, ZipItem metaDataItem) {
    78	            this.zipItemList = zipItemList;
    79	            this.metaDataItem = metaDataItem;
    80	        }
    81	        
    82	        public List<ZipItem> getZipItemList() {
    83	            return zipItemList;
    84	        }
    85	        
    86	        public void setZipItemList(List<ZipItem> zipItemList) {
    87	            this.zipItemList = zipItemList;
    88	        }
    89	        
    90	        public ZipItem getMetaDataItem() {
    91	            return metaDataItem;
    92	        }
    93	        
    94	        public void setMetaDataItem(ZipItem metaDataItem) {
    95	            this.metaDataItem = metaDataItem;
    96	        }
    97	    }
    98	    
    99	    /**
   100	     * zip method.
   101	     */
   102	    public static byte[] zip(List<ZipItem> source) {
   103	        byte[] result = null;
   104	        try (ByteArrayOutputStream byteOut = new ByteArrayOutputStream(); ZipOutputStream zipOut = new ZipOutputStream(
   105	                byteOut)) {
   106	            for (ZipItem item : source) {
   107	                zipOut.putNextEntry(new ZipEntry(item.getItemName()));
   108	                zipOut.write(item.getItemData().getBytes(StandardCharsets.UTF_8));
   109	            }
   110	            zipOut.flush();
   111	            zipOut.finish();
   112	            result = byteOut.toByteArray();
   113	        } catch (IOException e) {
   114	            LOGGER.error("an error occurred while compressing data.", e);
   115	        }
   116	        return result;
   117	    }
   118	    
   119	    /**
   120	     * unzip method.
   121	     */
   122	    public static UnZipResult unzip(byte[] source) {
   123	        List<ZipItem> itemList = new ArrayList<>();
   124	        ZipItem metaDataItem = null;
   125	        try (ZipInputStream zipIn = new ZipInputStream(new ByteArrayInputStream(source))) {
   126	            ZipEntry entry;
   127	            while ((entry = zipIn.getNextEntry()) != null) {
   128	                if (entry.isDirectory()) {
   129	                    continue;
   130	                }
   131	                try (ByteArrayOutputStream out = new ByteArrayOutputStream()) {
   132	                    byte[] buffer = new byte[1024];
   133	                    int offset;
   134	                    while ((offset = zipIn.read(buffer)) != -1) {
   135	                        out.write(buffer, 0, offset);
   136	                    }
   137	                    String entryName = entry.getName();
   138	                    if (metaDataItem == null && Constants.CONFIG_EXPORT_METADATA.equals(entryName)) {
   139	                        metaDataItem = new ZipItem(entryName, out.toString("UTF-8"));
   140	                        continue;
   141	                    }
   142	                    if (metaDataItem == null && Constants.CONFIG_EXPORT_METADATA_NEW.equals(entryName)) {
   143	                        metaDataItem = new ZipItem(entryName, out.toString("UTF-8"));
   144	                        continue;
   145	                    }
   146	                    itemList.add(new ZipItem(entryName, out.toString("UTF-8")));
   147	                } catch (IOException e) {
   148	                    LOGGER.error("unzip error", e);
   149	                }
   150	            }
   151	        } catch (IOException e) {
   152	            LOGGER.error("unzip error", e);
   153	        }
   154	        return new UnZipResult(itemList, metaDataItem);
   155	    }
   156	    
   157	}

    48

    78	            this.zipItemList = zipItemList;
    79	            this.metaDataItem = metaDataItem;

    98	    
    99	    /**
   100	     * zip method.
   101	     */
   102	    public static byte[] zip(List<ZipItem> source) {
   103	        byte[] result = null;
   104	        try (ByteArrayOutputStream byteOut = new ByteArrayOutputStream(); ZipOutputStream zipOut = new ZipOutputStream(
   105	                byteOut)) {
   106	            for (ZipItem item : source) {
   107	                zipOut.putNextEntry(new ZipEntry(item.getItemName()));
   108	                zipOut.write(item.getItemData().getBytes(StandardCharsets.UTF_8));
   109	            }
   110	            zipOut.flush();
   111	            zipOut.finish();
   112	            result = byteOut.toByteArray();
   113	        } catch (IOException e) {
   114	            LOGGER.error("an error occurred while compressing data.", e);
   115	        }
   116	        return result;
   117	    }
   118	    
   119	    /**
   120	     * unzip method.
   121	     */
   122	    public static UnZipResult unzip(byte[] source) {
   123	        List<ZipItem> itemList = new ArrayList<>();
   124	        ZipItem metaDataItem = null;
   125	        try (ZipInputStream zipIn = new ZipInputStream(new ByteArrayInputStream(source))) {
   126	            ZipEntry entry;
   127	            while ((entry = zipIn.getNextEntry()) != null) {
   128	                if (entry.isDirectory()) {
   129	                    continue;
   130	                }
   131	                try (ByteArrayOutputStream out = new ByteArrayOutputStream()) {
   132	                    byte[] buffer = new byte[1024];
   133	                    int offset;
   134	                    while ((offset = zipIn.read(buffer)) != -1) {
   135	                        out.write(buffer, 0, offset);
   136	                    }
   137	                    String entryName = entry.getName();
   138	                    if (metaDataItem == null && Constants.CONFIG_EXPORT_METADATA.equals(entryName)) {
   139	                        metaDataItem = new ZipItem(entryName, out.toString("UTF-8"));
   140	                        continue;
   141	                    }
   142	                    if (metaDataItem == null && Constants.CONFIG_EXPORT_METADATA_NEW.equals(entryName)) {
   143	                    if (metaDataItem == null && Constants.CONFIG_EXPORT_METADATA_OLD.equals(entryName)) {
   144	                        metaDataItem = new ZipItem(entryName, out.toString("UTF-8"));
   145	                        continue;
   146	                    }
   147	                        metaDataItem = new ZipItem(entryName, out.toString("UTF-8"));
   148	                        continue;
   149	                    }
   150	                    itemList.add(new ZipItem(entryName, out.toString("UTF-8")));
   151	                } catch (IOException e) {
   152	                    LOGGER.error("unzip error", e);
   153	                }
   154	            }
   155	        } catch (IOException e) {
   156	            LOGGER.error("unzip error", e);
   157	        }
   158	        return new UnZipResult(itemList, metaDataItem);
   159	    }
   160	    
   161	}

package com.alibaba.nacos.config.server.utils;

import com.alibaba.nacos.config.server.constant.Constants;
import org.slf4j.Logger;
import org.slf4j.LoggerFactory;

import java.io.ByteArrayInputStream;
import java.io.ByteArrayOutputStream;
import java.io.IOException;
import java.nio.charset.StandardCharsets;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.zip.ZipEntry;
import java.util.zip.ZipInputStream;
import java.util.zip.ZipOutputStream;

/**
 * ZipUtils for import and export.
 *
 * @author klw
 * @date 2019/5/14 16:59
 */
public class ZipUtils {
    
    private static final Logger LOGGER = LoggerFactory.getLogger(ZipUtils.class);
    
    public static class ZipItem {
        
        private String itemName;
        
        private String itemData;
        
        public ZipItem(String itemName, String itemData) {
            this.itemName = itemName;
            this.itemData = itemData;
        }
        
        public String getItemName() {
            return itemName;
        }
        
        public void setItemName(String itemName) {
            this.itemName = itemName;
        }
        
        public String getItemData() {
            return itemData;
        }
        
        public void setItemData(String itemData) {
            this.itemData = itemData;
        }
    }
    
    public static class UnZipResult {
        
        private List<ZipItem> zipItemList;
        
        private ZipItem metaDataItem;
        
        public UnZipResult(List<ZipItem> zipItemList, ZipItem metaDataItem) {
            this.zipItemList = zipItemList;
            this.metaDataItem = metaDataItem;
        }
        
        public List<ZipItem> getZipItemList() {
            return zipItemList;
        }
        
        public void setZipItemList(List<ZipItem> zipItemList) {
            this.zipItemList = zipItemList;
        }
        
        public ZipItem getMetaDataItem() {
            return metaDataItem;
        }
        
        public void setMetaDataItem(ZipItem metaDataItem) {
            this.metaDataItem = metaDataItem;
        }
    }
    
    /**
     * zip method.
     */
    public static byte[] zip(List<ZipItem> source) {
        byte[] result = null;
        try (ByteArrayOutputStream byteOut = new ByteArrayOutputStream(); ZipOutputStream zipOut = new ZipOutputStream(
                byteOut)) {
            for (ZipItem item : source) {
                zipOut.putNextEntry(new ZipEntry(item.getItemName()));
                zipOut.write(item.getItemData().getBytes(StandardCharsets.UTF_8));
            }
            zipOut.flush();
            zipOut.finish();
            result = byteOut.toByteArray();
        } catch (IOException e) {
            LOGGER.error("an error occurred while compressing data.", e);
        }
        return result;
    }
    
    /**
     * unzip method.
     */
    public static UnZipResult unzip(byte[] source) {
        List<ZipItem> itemList = new ArrayList<>();
        ZipItem metaDataItem = null;
        try (ZipInputStream zipIn = new ZipInputStream(new ByteArrayInputStream(source))) {
            ZipEntry entry;
            while ((entry = zipIn.getNextEntry()) != null) {
                if (entry.isDirectory()) {
                    continue;
                }
                try (ByteArrayOutputStream out = new ByteArrayOutputStream()) {
                    byte[] buffer = new byte[1024];
                    int offset;
                    while ((offset = zipIn.read(buffer)) != -1) {
                        out.write(buffer, 0, offset);
                    }
                    String entryName = entry.getName();
                    if (metaDataItem == null && Constants.CONFIG_EXPORT_METADATA.equals(entryName)) {
                        metaDataItem = new ZipItem(entryName, out.toString("UTF-8"));
                        continue;
                    }
                    if (metaDataItem == null && Constants.CONFIG_EXPORT_METADATA_NEW.equals(entryName)) {
                        metaDataItem = new ZipItem(entryName, out.toString("UTF-8"));
                        continue;
                    }
                    if (metaDataItem == null && Constants.CONFIG_EXPORT_METADATA_OLD.equals(entryName)) {
                        metaDataItem = new ZipItem(entryName, out.toString("UTF-8"));
                        continue;
                    }
                    itemList.add(new ZipItem(entryName, out.toString("UTF-8")));
                } catch (IOException e) {
                    LOGGER.error("unzip error", e);
                }
            }
        } catch (IOException e) {
            LOGGER.error("unzip error", e);
        }
        return new UnZipResult(itemList, metaDataItem);
    }
    
}

   661	        for (ConfigAllInfo ci : queryedDataList) {
   662	            ConfigCloneInfo paramBean = configBeansMap.get(ci.getId());
   663	            ConfigAllInfo ci4save = new ConfigAllInfo();
   664	            ci4save.setTenant(namespaceId);
   665	            ci4save.setType(ci.getType());
   666	            ci4save.setGroup((paramBean != null && StringUtils.isNotBlank(paramBean.getTargetGroupName()))
   667	                    ? paramBean.getTargetGroupName() : ci.getGroup());
   668	            ci4save.setDataId((paramBean != null && StringUtils.isNotBlank(paramBean.getTargetDataId()))
   669	                    ? paramBean.getTargetDataId() : ci.getDataId());
   670	            ci4save.setContent(ci.getContent());
   671	            if (StringUtils.isNotBlank(ci.getAppName())) {
   672	                ci4save.setAppName(ci.getAppName());
   673	            }
   674	            ci4save.setDesc(ci.getDesc());
   675	            ci4save.setEncryptedDataKey(
   676	                    ci.getEncryptedDataKey() == null ? StringUtils.EMPTY : ci.getEncryptedDataKey());
   677	            configInfoList4Clone.add(ci4save);
   678	        }
   679	        if (StringUtils.isBlank(srcUser)) {
   680	            srcUser = RequestUtil.getSrcUserName(request);
   681	        }
   682	        final String srcIp = getRemoteIp(request);
   683	        String requestIpApp = RequestUtil.getAppName(request);
   684	        final Timestamp time = TimeUtils.getCurrentTime();
   685	        Map<String, Object> saveResult = configInfoPersistService.batchInsertOrUpdate(configInfoList4Clone, srcUser,
   686	                srcIp, null, policy);
   687	        for (ConfigInfo configInfo : configInfoList4Clone) {
   688	            ConfigChangePublisher.notifyConfigChange(
   689	                    new ConfigDataChangeEvent(configInfo.getDataId(), configInfo.getGroup(), configInfo.getTenant(),
   690	                            time.getTime()));
   691	            ConfigTraceService.logPersistenceEvent(configInfo.getDataId(), configInfo.getGroup(),
   692	                    configInfo.getTenant(), requestIpApp, time.getTime(), InetUtils.getSelfIP(),
   693	                    ConfigTraceService.PERSISTENCE_EVENT, ConfigTraceService.PERSISTENCE_TYPE_PUB,
   694	                    configInfo.getContent());
   695	        }
   696	        
   697	        return Result.success(saveResult);
   698	    }

   496	     * Import config add .metadata.yml file.
   497	     */
   498	    private Result<Map<String, Object>> parseImportDataV2(String srcUser, ZipUtils.UnZipResult unziped,
   499	            List<ConfigAllInfo> configInfoList, List<Map<String, String>> unrecognizedList, String namespaceId) {
   500	        ZipUtils.ZipItem metaDataItem = unziped.getMetaDataItem();
   501	        String metaData = metaDataItem.getItemData();
   502	        Map<String, Object> failedData = new HashMap<>(4);
   503	        
   504	        ConfigMetadata configMetadata = YamlParserUtil.loadObject(metaData, ConfigMetadata.class);
   505	        if (configMetadata == null || CollectionUtils.isEmpty(configMetadata.getMetadata())) {
   506	            failedData.put("succCount", 0);
   507	            return Result.failure(ErrorCode.METADATA_ILLEGAL, failedData);
   508	        }
   509	        List<ConfigMetadata.ConfigExportItem> configExportItems = configMetadata.getMetadata();
   510	        // check config metadata
   511	        for (ConfigMetadata.ConfigExportItem configExportItem : configExportItems) {
   512	            if (StringUtils.isBlank(configExportItem.getDataId()) || StringUtils.isBlank(configExportItem.getGroup())
   513	                    || StringUtils.isBlank(configExportItem.getType())) {
   514	                failedData.put("succCount", 0);
   515	                return Result.failure(ErrorCode.METADATA_ILLEGAL, failedData);
   516	            }
   517	        }
   518	        
   519	        List<ZipUtils.ZipItem> zipItemList = unziped.getZipItemList();
   520	        Set<String> metaDataKeys = configExportItems.stream()
   521	                .map(metaItem -> GroupKey.getKey(metaItem.getDataId(), metaItem.getGroup()))
   522	                .collect(Collectors.toSet());
   523	        
   524	        Map<String, String> configContentMap = new HashMap<>(zipItemList.size());
   525	        int itemNameLength = 2;
   526	        zipItemList.forEach(item -> {
   527	            String itemName = item.getItemName();
   528	            String[] groupAdnDataId = itemName.split(Constants.CONFIG_EXPORT_ITEM_FILE_SEPARATOR);
   529	            if (groupAdnDataId.length != itemNameLength) {
   530	                Map<String, String> unrecognizedItem = new HashMap<>(2);
   531	                unrecognizedItem.put("itemName", item.getItemName());
   532	                unrecognizedList.add(unrecognizedItem);
   533	                return;
   534	            }
   535	            
   536	            String group = groupAdnDataId[0];
   537	            String dataId = groupAdnDataId[1];
   538	            String key = GroupKey.getKey(dataId, group);
   539	            // metadata does not contain config file
   540	            if (!metaDataKeys.contains(key)) {
   541	                Map<String, String> unrecognizedItem = new HashMap<>(2);
   542	                unrecognizedItem.put("itemName", "Item not found in metadata: " + item.getItemName());
   543	                unrecognizedList.add(unrecognizedItem);
   544	                return;
   545	            }
   546	            String itemData = item.getItemData();
   547	            configContentMap.put(key, itemData);
   548	        });
   549	        
   550	        for (ConfigMetadata.ConfigExportItem configExportItem : configExportItems) {
   551	            String dataId = configExportItem.getDataId();
   552	            String group = configExportItem.getGroup();
   553	            String content = configContentMap.get(GroupKey.getKey(dataId, group));
   554	            // config file not in metadata
   555	            if (content == null) {
   556	                Map<String, String> unrecognizedItem = new HashMap<>(2);
   557	                unrecognizedItem.put("itemName", "Item not found in file: " + group + "/" + dataId);
   558	                unrecognizedList.add(unrecognizedItem);
   559	                continue;
   560	            }
   561	            // encrypted
   562	            Pair<String, String> pair = EncryptionHandler.encryptHandler(dataId, content);
   563	            content = pair.getSecond();
   564	            
   565	            ConfigAllInfo ci = new ConfigAllInfo();
   566	            ci.setGroup(group);
   567	            ci.setDataId(dataId);
   568	            ci.setContent(content);
   569	            ci.setType(configExportItem.getType());
   570	            ci.setDesc(configExportItem.getDesc());
   571	            ci.setAppName(configExportItem.getAppName());
   572	            ci.setTenant(namespaceId);
   573	            ci.setEncryptedDataKey(pair.getFirst());
   574	            ci.setCreateUser(srcUser);
   575	            configInfoList.add(ci);
   576	        }
   577	        
   578	        return null;
   579	    }

    /**
     * Import config add .metadata.yml file.
     */
    private Result<Map<String, Object>> parseImportDataV2(String srcUser, ZipUtils.UnZipResult unziped,
            List<ConfigAllInfo> configInfoList, List<Map<String, String>> unrecognizedList, String namespaceId) {
        ZipUtils.ZipItem metaDataItem = unziped.getMetaDataItem();
        Map<String, Object> failedData = new HashMap<>(4);
        
        if (metaDataItem == null) {
            failedData.put("succCount", 0);
            return Result.failure(ErrorCode.METADATA_ILLEGAL, failedData);
        }
        
        String metaData = metaDataItem.getItemData();
        
        // Try to parse as YAML format (.metadata.yml or .meta.yml)
        ConfigMetadata configMetadata = YamlParserUtil.loadObject(metaData, ConfigMetadata.class);
        if (configMetadata != null && !CollectionUtils.isEmpty(configMetadata.getMetadata())) {
            return processMetadataV2(srcUser, unziped, configInfoList, unrecognizedList, namespaceId, configMetadata);
        }
        
        // Try to parse as old pipe-separated format (meta_data)
        if (Constants.CONFIG_EXPORT_METADATA_OLD.equals(metaDataItem.getItemName())) {
            return processMetadataOldFormat(srcUser, unziped, configInfoList, unrecognizedList, namespaceId, metaData);
        }
        
        failedData.put("succCount", 0);
        return Result.failure(ErrorCode.METADATA_ILLEGAL, failedData);
    }
    
    private Result<Map<String, Object>> processMetadataV2(String srcUser, ZipUtils.UnZipResult unziped,
            List<ConfigAllInfo> configInfoList, List<Map<String, String>> unrecognizedList, String namespaceId,
            ConfigMetadata configMetadata) {
        Map<String, Object> failedData = new HashMap<>(4);
        List<ConfigMetadata.ConfigExportItem> configExportItems = configMetadata.getMetadata();
        // check config metadata
        for (ConfigMetadata.ConfigExportItem configExportItem : configExportItems) {
            if (StringUtils.isBlank(configExportItem.getDataId()) || StringUtils.isBlank(configExportItem.getGroup())
                    || StringUtils.isBlank(configExportItem.getType())) {
                failedData.put("succCount", 0);
                return Result.failure(ErrorCode.METADATA_ILLEGAL, failedData);
            }
        }
        
        List<ZipUtils.ZipItem> zipItemList = unziped.getZipItemList();
        Set<String> metaDataKeys = configExportItems.stream()
                .map(metaItem -> GroupKey.getKey(metaItem.getDataId(), metaItem.getGroup()))
                .collect(Collectors.toSet());
        
        Map<String, String> configContentMap = new HashMap<>(zipItemList.size());
        int itemNameLength = 2;
        zipItemList.forEach(item -> {
            String itemName = item.getItemName();
            String[] groupAdnDataId = itemName.split(Constants.CONFIG_EXPORT_ITEM_FILE_SEPARATOR);
            if (groupAdnDataId.length != itemNameLength) {
                Map<String, String> unrecognizedItem = new HashMap<>(2);
                unrecognizedItem.put("itemName", item.getItemName());
                unrecognizedList.add(unrecognizedItem);
                return;
            }
            
            String group = groupAdnDataId[0];
            String dataId = groupAdnDataId[1];
            String key = GroupKey.getKey(dataId, group);
            // metadata does not contain config file
            if (!metaDataKeys.contains(key)) {
                Map<String, String> unrecognizedItem = new HashMap<>(2);
                unrecognizedItem.put("itemName", "Item not found in metadata: " + item.getItemName());
                unrecognizedList.add(unrecognizedItem);
                return;
            }
            String itemData = item.getItemData();
            configContentMap.put(key, itemData);
        });
        
        for (ConfigMetadata.ConfigExportItem configExportItem : configExportItems) {
            String dataId = configExportItem.getDataId();
            String group = configExportItem.getGroup();
            String content = configContentMap.get(GroupKey.getKey(dataId, group));
            // config file not in metadata
            if (content == null) {
                Map<String, String> unrecognizedItem = new HashMap<>(2);
                unrecognizedItem.put("itemName", "Item not found in file: " + group + "/" + dataId);
                unrecognizedList.add(unrecognizedItem);
                continue;
            }
            // encrypted
            Pair<String, String> pair = EncryptionHandler.encryptHandler(dataId, content);
            content = pair.getSecond();
            
            ConfigAllInfo ci = new ConfigAllInfo();
            ci.setGroup(group);
            ci.setDataId(dataId);
            ci.setContent(content);
            ci.setType(configExportItem.getType());
            ci.setDesc(configExportItem.getDesc());
            ci.setAppName(configExportItem.getAppName());
            ci.setTenant(namespaceId);
            ci.setEncryptedDataKey(pair.getFirst());
            ci.setCreateUser(srcUser);
            configInfoList.add(ci);
        }
        
        return null;
    }
    
    private Result<Map<String, Object>> processMetadataOldFormat(String srcUser, ZipUtils.UnZipResult unziped,
            List<ConfigAllInfo> configInfoList, List<Map<String, String>> unrecognizedList, String namespaceId,
            String metaData) {
        Map<String, Object> failedData = new HashMap<>(4);
        
        // Old format: each line is "GROUP|dataId|tenantId"
        String[] lines = metaData.split("\\r?\\n");
        List<ZipUtils.ZipItem> zipItemList = unziped.getZipItemList();
        
        // Build a map of group/dataId to zip item
        Map<String, ZipUtils.ZipItem> itemMap = new HashMap<>(zipItemList.size());
        int itemNameLength = 2;
        for (ZipUtils.ZipItem item : zipItemList) {
            String itemName = item.getItemName();
            String[] groupAdnDataId = itemName.split(Constants.CONFIG_EXPORT_ITEM_FILE_SEPARATOR);
            if (groupAdnDataId.length != itemNameLength) {
                Map<String, String> unrecognizedItem = new HashMap<>(2);
                unrecognizedItem.put("itemName", item.getItemName());
                unrecognizedList.add(unrecognizedItem);
                continue;
            }
            String group = groupAdnDataId[0];
            String dataId = groupAdnDataId[1];
            String key = GroupKey.getKey(dataId, group);
            itemMap.put(key, item);
        }
        
        for (String line : lines) {
            if (StringUtils.isBlank(line)) {
                continue;
            }
            String[] parts = line.split("\\|");
            if (parts.length < 2) {
                continue;
            }
            String group = parts[0];
            String dataId = parts[1];
            String tenantId = parts.length > 2 ? parts[2] : "";
            
            String key = GroupKey.getKey(dataId, group);
            ZipUtils.ZipItem item = itemMap.get(key);
            if (item == null) {
                Map<String, String> unrecognizedItem = new HashMap<>(2);
                unrecognizedItem.put("itemName", "Item not found in file: " + group + "/" + dataId);
                unrecognizedList.add(unrecognizedItem);
                continue;
            }
            
            String content = item.getItemData();
            // encrypted
            Pair<String, String> pair = EncryptionHandler.encryptHandler(dataId, content);
            content = pair.getSecond();
            
            ConfigAllInfo ci = new ConfigAllInfo();
            ci.setGroup(group);
            ci.setDataId(dataId);
            ci.setContent(content);
            ci.setType("text");
            ci.setTenant(StringUtils.isBlank(tenantId) ? namespaceId : tenantId);
            ci.setEncryptedDataKey(pair.getFirst());
            ci.setCreateUser(srcUser);
            configInfoList.add(ci);
        }
        
        return null;
    }
EOF

    /**
     * Import config add .metadata.yml file.
     */
    private Result<Map<String, Object>> parseImportDataV2(String srcUser, ZipUtils.UnZipResult unziped,
            List<ConfigAllInfo> configInfoList, List<Map<String, String>> unrecognizedList, String namespaceId) {
        ZipUtils.ZipItem metaDataItem = unziped.getMetaDataItem();
        String metaData = metaDataItem.getItemData();
        Map<String, Object> failedData = new HashMap<>(4);
        
        ConfigMetadata configMetadata = YamlParserUtil.loadObject(metaData, ConfigMetadata.class);
        if (configMetadata == null || CollectionUtils.isEmpty(configMetadata.getMetadata())) {
            failedData.put("succCount", 0);
            return Result.failure(ErrorCode.METADATA_ILLEGAL, failedData);
        }
        List<ConfigMetadata.ConfigExportItem> configExportItems = configMetadata.getMetadata();
        // check config metadata
        for (ConfigMetadata.ConfigExportItem configExportItem : configExportItems) {
            if (StringUtils.isBlank(configExportItem.getDataId()) || StringUtils.isBlank(configExportItem.getGroup())
                    || StringUtils.isBlank(configExportItem.getType())) {
                failedData.put("succCount", 0);
                return Result.failure(ErrorCode.METADATA_ILLEGAL, failedData);
            }
        }
        
        List<ZipUtils.ZipItem> zipItemList = unziped.getZipItemList();
        Set<String> metaDataKeys = configExportItems.stream()
                .map(metaItem -> GroupKey.getKey(metaItem.getDataId(), metaItem.getGroup()))
                .collect(Collectors.toSet());
        
        Map<String, String> configContentMap = new HashMap<>(zipItemList.size());
        int itemNameLength = 2;
        zipItemList.forEach(item -> {
            String itemName = item.getItemName();
            String[] groupAdnDataId = itemName.split(Constants.CONFIG_EXPORT_ITEM_FILE_SEPARATOR);
            if (groupAdnDataId.length != itemNameLength) {
                Map<String, String> unrecognizedItem = new HashMap<>(2);
                unrecognizedItem.put("itemName", item.getItemName());
                unrecognizedList.add(unrecognizedItem);
                return;
            }
            
            String group = groupAdnDataId[0];
            String dataId = groupAdnDataId[1];
            String key = GroupKey.getKey(dataId, group);
            // metadata does not contain config file
            if (!metaDataKeys.contains(key)) {
                Map<String, String> unrecognizedItem = new HashMap<>(2);
                unrecognizedItem.put("itemName", "Item not found in metadata: " + item.getItemName());
                unrecognizedList.add(unrecognizedItem);
                return;
            }
            String itemData = item.getItemData();
            configContentMap.put(key, itemData);
        });
        
        for (ConfigMetadata.ConfigExportItem configExportItem : configExportItems) {
            String dataId = configExportItem.getDataId();
            String group = configExportItem.getGroup();
            String content = configContentMap.get(GroupKey.getKey(dataId, group));
            // config file not in metadata
            if (content == null) {
                Map<String, String> unrecognizedItem = new HashMap<>(2);
                unrecognizedItem.put("itemName", "Item not found in file: " + group + "/" + dataId);
                unrecognizedList.add(unrecognizedItem);
                continue;
            }
            // encrypted
            Pair<String, String> pair = EncryptionHandler.encryptHandler(dataId, content);
            content = pair.getSecond();
            
            ConfigAllInfo ci = new ConfigAllInfo();
            ci.setGroup(group);
            ci.setDataId(dataId);
            ci.setContent(content);
            ci.setType(configExportItem.getType());
            ci.setDesc(configExportItem.getDesc());
            ci.setAppName(configExportItem.getAppName());
            ci.setTenant(namespaceId);
            ci.setEncryptedDataKey(pair.getFirst());
            ci.setCreateUser(srcUser);
            configInfoList.add(ci);
        }
        
        return null;
    }
