old_method = '''    /**
     * Import config add .metadata.yml file.
     */
    private Result<Map<String, Object>> parseImportDataV2(String srcUser, ZipUtils.UnZipResult unziped,
            List<ConfigAllInfo> configInfoList, List<Map<String, String>> unrecognizedList, String namespaceId) {
        ZipUtils.ZipItem metaDataItem = unziped.getMetaDataItem();
        String metaData = metaDataItem.getItemData();
        Map<String, Object> failedData = new HashMap<>(4);
        
        ConfigMetadata configMetadata = YamlParserUtil.loadObject(metaData, ConfigMetadata.class);
        if (configMetadata == null || CollectionUtils.isEmpty(configMetadata.getMetadata())) {
            failedData.put("succCount", 0);
            return Result.failure(ErrorCode.METADATA_ILLEGAL, failedData);
        }
        List<ConfigMetadata.ConfigExportItem> configExportItems = configMetadata.getMetadata();
        // check config metadata
        for (ConfigMetadata.ConfigExportItem configExportItem : configExportItems) {
            if (StringUtils.isBlank(configExportItem.getDataId()) || StringUtils.isBlank(configExportItem.getGroup())
                    || StringUtils.isBlank(configExportItem.getType())) {
                failedData.put("succCount", 0);
                return Result.failure(ErrorCode.METADATA_ILLEGAL, failedData);
            }
        }
        
        List<ZipUtils.ZipItem> zipItemList = unziped.getZipItemList();
        Set<String> metaDataKeys = configExportItems.stream()
                .map(metaItem -> GroupKey.getKey(metaItem.getDataId(), metaItem.getGroup()))
                .collect(Collectors.toSet());
        
        Map<String, String> configContentMap = new HashMap<>(zipItemList.size());
        int itemNameLength = 2;
        zipItemList.forEach(item -> {
            String itemName = item.getItemName();
            String[] groupAdnDataId = itemName.split(Constants.CONFIG_EXPORT_ITEM_FILE_SEPARATOR);
            if (groupAdnDataId.length != itemNameLength) {
                Map<String, String> unrecognizedItem = new HashMap<>(2);
                unrecognizedItem.put("itemName", item.getItemName());
                unrecognizedList.add(unrecognizedItem);
                return;
            }
            
            String group = groupAdnDataId[0];
            String dataId = groupAdnDataId[1];
            String key = GroupKey.getKey(dataId, group);
            // metadata does not contain config file
            if (!metaDataKeys.contains(key)) {
                Map<String, String> unrecognizedItem = new HashMap<>(2);
                unrecognizedItem.put("itemName", "Item not found in metadata: " + item.getItemName());
                unrecognizedList.add(unrecognizedItem);
                return;
            }
            String itemData = item.getItemData();
            configContentMap.put(key, itemData);
        });
        
        for (ConfigMetadata.ConfigExportItem configExportItem : configExportItems) {
            String dataId = configExportItem.getDataId();
            String group = configExportItem.getGroup();
            String content = configContentMap.get(GroupKey.getKey(dataId, group));
            // config file not in metadata
            if (content == null) {
                Map<String, String> unrecognizedItem = new HashMap<>(2);
                unrecognizedItem.put("itemName", "Item not found in file: " + group + "/" + dataId);
                unrecognizedList.add(unrecognizedItem);
                continue;
            }
            // encrypted
            Pair<String, String> pair = EncryptionHandler.encryptHandler(dataId, content);
            content = pair.getSecond();
            
            ConfigAllInfo ci = new ConfigAllInfo();
            ci.setGroup(group);
            ci.setDataId(dataId);
            ci.setContent(content);
            ci.setType(configExportItem.getType());
            ci.setDesc(configExportItem.getDesc());
            ci.setAppName(configExportItem.getAppName());
            ci.setTenant(namespaceId);
            ci.setEncryptedDataKey(pair.getFirst());
            ci.setCreateUser(srcUser);
            configInfoList.add(ci);
        }
        
        return null;
    }'''

new_method = '''    /**
     * Import config add .metadata.yml file.
     */
    private Result<Map<String, Object>> parseImportDataV2(String srcUser, ZipUtils.UnZipResult unziped,
            List<ConfigAllInfo> configInfoList, List<Map<String, String>> unrecognizedList, String namespaceId) {
        ZipUtils.ZipItem metaDataItem = unziped.getMetaDataItem();
        Map<String, Object> failedData = new HashMap<>(4);
        
        if (metaDataItem == null) {
            failedData.put("succCount", 0);
            return Result.failure(ErrorCode.METADATA_ILLEGAL, failedData);
        }
        
        String metaData = metaDataItem.getItemData();
        
        // Try to parse as YAML format (.metadata.yml or .meta.yml)
        ConfigMetadata configMetadata = YamlParserUtil.loadObject(metaData, ConfigMetadata.class);
        if (configMetadata != null && !CollectionUtils.isEmpty(configMetadata.getMetadata())) {
            return processMetadataV2(srcUser, unziped, configInfoList, unrecognizedList, namespaceId, configMetadata);
        }
        
        // Try to parse as old pipe-separated format (meta_data)
        if (Constants.CONFIG_EXPORT_METADATA_OLD.equals(metaDataItem.getItemName())) {
            return processMetadataOldFormat(srcUser, unziped, configInfoList, unrecognizedList, namespaceId, metaData);
        }
        
        failedData.put("succCount", 0);
        return Result.failure(ErrorCode.METADATA_ILLEGAL, failedData);
    }
    
    private Result<Map<String, Object>> processMetadataV2(String srcUser, ZipUtils.UnZipResult unziped,
            List<ConfigAllInfo> configInfoList, List<Map<String, String>> unrecognizedList, String namespaceId,
            ConfigMetadata configMetadata) {
        Map<String, Object> failedData = new HashMap<>(4);
        List<ConfigMetadata.ConfigExportItem> configExportItems = configMetadata.getMetadata();
        // check config metadata
        for (ConfigMetadata.ConfigExportItem configExportItem : configExportItems) {
            if (StringUtils.isBlank(configExportItem.getDataId()) || StringUtils.isBlank(configExportItem.getGroup())
                    || StringUtils.isBlank(configExportItem.getType())) {
                failedData.put("succCount", 0);
                return Result.failure(ErrorCode.METADATA_ILLEGAL, failedData);
            }
        }
        
        List<ZipUtils.ZipItem> zipItemList = unziped.getZipItemList();
        Set<String> metaDataKeys = configExportItems.stream()
                .map(metaItem -> GroupKey.getKey(metaItem.getDataId(), metaItem.getGroup()))
                .collect(Collectors.toSet());
        
        Map<String, String> configContentMap = new HashMap<>(zipItemList.size());
        int itemNameLength = 2;
        zipItemList.forEach(item -> {
            String itemName = item.getItemName();
            String[] groupAdnDataId = itemName.split(Constants.CONFIG_EXPORT_ITEM_FILE_SEPARATOR);
            if (groupAdnDataId.length != itemNameLength) {
                Map<String, String> unrecognizedItem = new HashMap<>(2);
                unrecognizedItem.put("itemName", item.getItemName());
                unrecognizedList.add(unrecognizedItem);
                return;
            }
            
            String group = groupAdnDataId[0];
            String dataId = groupAdnDataId[1];
            String key = GroupKey.getKey(dataId, group);
            // metadata does not contain config file
            if (!metaDataKeys.contains(key)) {
                Map<String, String> unrecognizedItem = new HashMap<>(2);
                unrecognizedItem.put("itemName", "Item not found in metadata: " + item.getItemName());
                unrecognizedList.add(unrecognizedItem);
                return;
            }
            String itemData = item.getItemData();
            configContentMap.put(key, itemData);
        });
        
        for (ConfigMetadata.ConfigExportItem configExportItem : configExportItems) {
            String dataId = configExportItem.getDataId();
            String group = configExportItem.getGroup();
            String content = configContentMap.get(GroupKey.getKey(dataId, group));
            // config file not in metadata
            if (content == null) {
                Map<String, String> unrecognizedItem = new HashMap<>(2);
                unrecognizedItem.put("itemName", "Item not found in file: " + group + "/" + dataId);
                unrecognizedList.add(unrecognizedItem);
                continue;
            }
            // encrypted
            Pair<String, String> pair = EncryptionHandler.encryptHandler(dataId, content);
            content = pair.getSecond();
            
            ConfigAllInfo ci = new ConfigAllInfo();
            ci.setGroup(group);
            ci.setDataId(dataId);
            ci.setContent(content);
            ci.setType(configExportItem.getType());
            ci.setDesc(configExportItem.getDesc());
            ci.setAppName(configExportItem.getAppName());
            ci.setTenant(namespaceId);
            ci.setEncryptedDataKey(pair.getFirst());
            ci.setCreateUser(srcUser);
            configInfoList.add(ci);
        }
        
        return null;
    }
    
    private Result<Map<String, Object>> processMetadataOldFormat(String srcUser, ZipUtils.UnZipResult unziped,
            List<ConfigAllInfo> configInfoList, List<Map<String, String>> unrecognizedList, String namespaceId,
            String metaData) {
        Map<String, Object> failedData = new HashMap<>(4);
        
        // Old format: each line is "GROUP|dataId|tenantId"
        String[] lines = metaData.split("\\\\r?\\\\n");
        List<ZipUtils.ZipItem> zipItemList = unziped.getZipItemList();
        
        // Build a map of group/dataId to zip item
        Map<String, ZipUtils.ZipItem> itemMap = new HashMap<>(zipItemList.size());
        int itemNameLength = 2;
        for (ZipUtils.ZipItem item : zipItemList) {
            String itemName = item.getItemName();
            String[] groupAdnDataId = itemName.split(Constants.CONFIG_EXPORT_ITEM_FILE_SEPARATOR);
            if (groupAdnDataId.length != itemNameLength) {
                Map<String, String> unrecognizedItem = new HashMap<>(2);
                unrecognizedItem.put("itemName", item.getItemName());
                unrecognizedList.add(unrecognizedItem);
                continue;
            }
            String group = groupAdnDataId[0];
            String dataId = groupAdnDataId[1];
            String key = GroupKey.getKey(dataId, group);
            itemMap.put(key, item);
        }
        
        for (String line : lines) {
            if (StringUtils.isBlank(line)) {
                continue;
            }
            String[] parts = line.split("\\\\|");
            if (parts.length < 2) {
                continue;
            }
            String group = parts[0];
            String dataId = parts[1];
            String tenantId = parts.length > 2 ? parts[2] : "";
            
            String key = GroupKey.getKey(dataId, group);
            ZipUtils.ZipItem item = itemMap.get(key);
            if (item == null) {
                Map<String, String> unrecognizedItem = new HashMap<>(2);
                unrecognizedItem.put("itemName", "Item not found in file: " + group + "/" + dataId);
                unrecognizedList.add(unrecognizedItem);
                continue;
            }
            
            String content = item.getItemData();
            // encrypted
            Pair<String, String> pair = EncryptionHandler.encryptHandler(dataId, content);
            content = pair.getSecond();
            
            ConfigAllInfo ci = new ConfigAllInfo();
            ci.setGroup(group);
            ci.setDataId(dataId);
            ci.setContent(content);
            ci.setType("text");
            ci.setTenant(StringUtils.isBlank(tenantId) ? namespaceId : tenantId);
            ci.setEncryptedDataKey(pair.getFirst());
            ci.setCreateUser(srcUser);
            configInfoList.add(ci);
        }
        
        return null;
    }'''

if old_method in content:

import sys

# Read the file
with open('/testbed/console/src/main/java/com/alibaba/nacos/console/handler/impl/inner/config/ConfigInnerHandler.java', 'r') as f:

old_method = '''    /**
     * new version import config add .metadata.yml file.
     *
     * @param unziped          export file.
     * @param configInfoList   parse file result.
     * @param unrecognizedList unrecognized file.
     * @param namespace        import namespace.
     * @return error result.
     */
    private Result<Map<String, Object>> parseImportDataV2(String srcUser, ZipUtils.UnZipResult unziped,
            List<ConfigAllInfo> configInfoList, List<Map<String, String>> unrecognizedList, String namespace) {
        ZipUtils.ZipItem metaDataItem = unziped.getMetaDataItem();
        String metaData = metaDataItem.getItemData();
        Map<String, Object> failedData = new HashMap<>(4);
        
        ConfigMetadata configMetadata = YamlParserUtil.loadObject(metaData, ConfigMetadata.class);
        if (configMetadata == null || CollectionUtils.isEmpty(configMetadata.getMetadata())) {
            failedData.put("succCount", 0);
            return Result.failure(ErrorCode.METADATA_ILLEGAL, failedData);
        }
        List<ConfigMetadata.ConfigExportItem> configExportItems = configMetadata.getMetadata();
        // check config metadata
        for (ConfigMetadata.ConfigExportItem configExportItem : configExportItems) {
            if (StringUtils.isBlank(configExportItem.getDataId()) || StringUtils.isBlank(configExportItem.getGroup())
                    || StringUtils.isBlank(configExportItem.getType())) {
                failedData.put("succCount", 0);
                return Result.failure(ErrorCode.METADATA_ILLEGAL, failedData);
            }
        }
        
        List<ZipUtils.ZipItem> zipItemList = unziped.getZipItemList();
        Set<String> metaDataKeys = configExportItems.stream()
                .map(metaItem -> GroupKey.getKey(metaItem.getDataId(), metaItem.getGroup()))
                .collect(Collectors.toSet());
        
        Map<String, String> configContentMap = new HashMap<>(zipItemList.size());
        int itemNameLength = 2;
        zipItemList.forEach(item -> {
            String itemName = item.getItemName();
            String[] groupAdnDataId = itemName.split(Constants.CONFIG_EXPORT_ITEM_FILE_SEPARATOR);
            if (groupAdnDataId.length != itemNameLength) {
                Map<String, String> unrecognizedItem = new HashMap<>(2);
                unrecognizedItem.put("itemName", item.getItemName());
                unrecognizedList.add(unrecognizedItem);
                return;
            }
            
            String group = groupAdnDataId[0];
            String dataId = groupAdnDataId[1];
            String key = GroupKey.getKey(dataId, group);
            // metadata does not contain config file
            if (!metaDataKeys.contains(key)) {
                Map<String, String> unrecognizedItem = new HashMap<>(2);
                unrecognizedItem.put("itemName", "未在元数据中找到: " + item.getItemName());
                unrecognizedList.add(unrecognizedItem);
                return;
            }
            String itemData = item.getItemData();
            configContentMap.put(key, itemData);
        });
        
        for (ConfigMetadata.ConfigExportItem configExportItem : configExportItems) {
            String dataId = configExportItem.getDataId();
            String group = configExportItem.getGroup();
            String content = configContentMap.get(GroupKey.getKey(dataId, group));
            // config file not in metadata
            if (content == null) {
                Map<String, String> unrecognizedItem = new HashMap<>(2);
                unrecognizedItem.put("itemName", "未在文件中找到: " + group + "/" + dataId);
                unrecognizedList.add(unrecognizedItem);
                continue;
            }
            // encrypted
            Pair<String, String> pair = EncryptionHandler.encryptHandler(dataId, content);
            content = pair.getSecond();
            
            ConfigAllInfo ci = new ConfigAllInfo();
            ci.setGroup(group);
            ci.setDataId(dataId);
            ci.setContent(content);
            ci.setType(configExportItem.getType());
            ci.setDesc(configExportItem.getDesc());
            ci.setAppName(configExportItem.getAppName());
            ci.setTenant(namespace);
            ci.setEncryptedDataKey(pair.getFirst());
            ci.setCreateUser(srcUser);
            configInfoList.add(ci);
        }
        return null;
    }'''

new_method = '''    /**
     * new version import config add .metadata.yml file.
     *
     * @param unziped          export file.
     * @param configInfoList   parse file result.
     * @param unrecognizedList unrecognized file.
     * @param namespace        import namespace.
     * @return error result.
     */
    private Result<Map<String, Object>> parseImportDataV2(String srcUser, ZipUtils.UnZipResult unziped,
            List<ConfigAllInfo> configInfoList, List<Map<String, String>> unrecognizedList, String namespace) {
        ZipUtils.ZipItem metaDataItem = unziped.getMetaDataItem();
        Map<String, Object> failedData = new HashMap<>(4);
        
        if (metaDataItem == null) {
            failedData.put("succCount", 0);
            return Result.failure(ErrorCode.METADATA_ILLEGAL, failedData);
        }
        
        String metaData = metaDataItem.getItemData();
        
        // Try to parse as YAML format (.metadata.yml or .meta.yml)
        ConfigMetadata configMetadata = YamlParserUtil.loadObject(metaData, ConfigMetadata.class);
        if (configMetadata != null && !CollectionUtils.isEmpty(configMetadata.getMetadata())) {
            return processMetadataV2(srcUser, unziped, configInfoList, unrecognizedList, namespace, configMetadata);
        }
        
        // Try to parse as old pipe-separated format (meta_data)
        if (Constants.CONFIG_EXPORT_METADATA_OLD.equals(metaDataItem.getItemName())) {
            return processMetadataOldFormat(srcUser, unziped, configInfoList, unrecognizedList, namespace, metaData);
        }
        
        failedData.put("succCount", 0);
        return Result.failure(ErrorCode.METADATA_ILLEGAL, failedData);
    }
    
    private Result<Map<String, Object>> processMetadataV2(String srcUser, ZipUtils.UnZipResult unziped,
            List<ConfigAllInfo> configInfoList, List<Map<String, String>> unrecognizedList, String namespace,
            ConfigMetadata configMetadata) {
        Map<String, Object> failedData = new HashMap<>(4);
        List<ConfigMetadata.ConfigExportItem> configExportItems = configMetadata.getMetadata();
        // check config metadata
        for (ConfigMetadata.ConfigExportItem configExportItem : configExportItems) {
            if (StringUtils.isBlank(configExportItem.getDataId()) || StringUtils.isBlank(configExportItem.getGroup())
                    || StringUtils.isBlank(configExportItem.getType())) {
                failedData.put("succCount", 0);
                return Result.failure(ErrorCode.METADATA_ILLEGAL, failedData);
            }
        }
        
        List<ZipUtils.ZipItem> zipItemList = unziped.getZipItemList();
        Set<String> metaDataKeys = configExportItems.stream()
                .map(metaItem -> GroupKey.getKey(metaItem.getDataId(), metaItem.getGroup()))
                .collect(Collectors.toSet());
        
        Map<String, String> configContentMap = new HashMap<>(zipItemList.size());
        int itemNameLength = 2;
        zipItemList.forEach(item -> {
            String itemName = item.getItemName();
            String[] groupAdnDataId = itemName.split(Constants.CONFIG_EXPORT_ITEM_FILE_SEPARATOR);
            if (groupAdnDataId.length != itemNameLength) {
                Map<String, String> unrecognizedItem = new HashMap<>(2);
                unrecognizedItem.put("itemName", item.getItemName());
                unrecognizedList.add(unrecognizedItem);
                return;
            }
            
            String group = groupAdnDataId[0];
            String dataId = groupAdnDataId[1];
            String key = GroupKey.getKey(dataId, group);
            // metadata does not contain config file
            if (!metaDataKeys.contains(key)) {
                Map<String, String> unrecognizedItem = new HashMap<>(2);
                unrecognizedItem.put("itemName", "Item not found in metadata: " + item.getItemName());
                unrecognizedList.add(unrecognizedItem);
                return;
            }
            String itemData = item.getItemData();
            configContentMap.put(key, itemData);
        });
        
        for (ConfigMetadata.ConfigExportItem configExportItem : configExportItems) {
            String dataId = configExportItem.getDataId();
            String group = configExportItem.getGroup();
            String content = configContentMap.get(GroupKey.getKey(dataId, group));
            // config file not in metadata
            if (content == null) {
                Map<String, String> unrecognizedItem = new HashMap<>(2);
                unrecognizedItem.put("itemName", "Item not found in file: " + group + "/" + dataId);
                unrecognizedList.add(unrecognizedItem);
                continue;
            }
            // encrypted
            Pair<String, String> pair = EncryptionHandler.encryptHandler(dataId, content);
            content = pair.getSecond();
            
            ConfigAllInfo ci = new ConfigAllInfo();
            ci.setGroup(group);
            ci.setDataId(dataId);
            ci.setContent(content);
            ci.setType(configExportItem.getType());
            ci.setDesc(configExportItem.getDesc());
            ci.setAppName(configExportItem.getAppName());
            ci.setTenant(namespace);
            ci.setEncryptedDataKey(pair.getFirst());
            ci.setCreateUser(srcUser);
            configInfoList.add(ci);
        }
        return null;
    }
    
    private Result<Map<String, Object>> processMetadataOldFormat(String srcUser, ZipUtils.UnZipResult unziped,
            List<ConfigAllInfo> configInfoList, List<Map<String, String>> unrecognizedList, String namespace,
            String metaData) {
        Map<String, Object> failedData = new HashMap<>(4);
        
        // Old format: each line is "GROUP|dataId|tenantId"
        String[] lines = metaData.split("\\\\r?\\\\n");
        List<ZipUtils.ZipItem> zipItemList = unziped.getZipItemList();
        
        // Build a map of group/dataId to zip item
        Map<String, ZipUtils.ZipItem> itemMap = new HashMap<>(zipItemList.size());
        int itemNameLength = 2;
        for (ZipUtils.ZipItem item : zipItemList) {
            String itemName = item.getItemName();
            String[] groupAdnDataId = itemName.split(Constants.CONFIG_EXPORT_ITEM_FILE_SEPARATOR);
            if (groupAdnDataId.length != itemNameLength) {
                Map<String, String> unrecognizedItem = new HashMap<>(2);
                unrecognizedItem.put("itemName", item.getItemName());
                unrecognizedList.add(unrecognizedItem);
                continue;
            }
            String group = groupAdnDataId[0];
            String dataId = groupAdnDataId[1];
            String key = GroupKey.getKey(dataId, group);
            itemMap.put(key, item);
        }
        
        for (String line : lines) {
            if (StringUtils.isBlank(line)) {
                continue;
            }
            String[] parts = line.split("\\\\|");
            if (parts.length < 2) {
                continue;
            }
            String group = parts[0];
            String dataId = parts[1];
            String tenantId = parts.length > 2 ? parts[2] : "";
            
            String key = GroupKey.getKey(dataId, group);
            ZipUtils.ZipItem item = itemMap.get(key);
            if (item == null) {
                Map<String, String> unrecognizedItem = new HashMap<>(2);
                unrecognizedItem.put("itemName", "Item not found in file: " + group + "/" + dataId);
                unrecognizedList.add(unrecognizedItem);
                continue;
            }
            
            String content = item.getItemData();
            // encrypted
            Pair<String, String> pair = EncryptionHandler.encryptHandler(dataId, content);
            content = pair.getSecond();
            
            ConfigAllInfo ci = new ConfigAllInfo();
            ci.setGroup(group);
            ci.setDataId(dataId);
            ci.setContent(content);
            ci.setType("text");
            ci.setTenant(StringUtils.isBlank(tenantId) ? namespace : tenantId);
            ci.setEncryptedDataKey(pair.getFirst());
            ci.setCreateUser(srcUser);
            configInfoList.add(ci);
        }
        
        return null;
    }'''

if old_method in content:
    content = content.replace(old_method, new_method)
    with open('/testbed/console/src/main/java/com/alibaba/nacos/console/handler/impl/inner/config/ConfigInnerHandler.java', 'w') as f:
        f.write(content)
    print("SUCCESS: ConfigInnerHandler.java updated")

        print("Method not found at all!")

    18	
    19	import com.alibaba.nacos.config.server.constant.Constants;
    20	import org.slf4j.Logger;
    21	import org.slf4j.LoggerFactory;
    22	
    23	import java.io.ByteArrayInputStream;
    24	import java.io.ByteArrayOutputStream;
    25	import java.io.IOException;
    26	import java.nio.charset.StandardCharsets;
    27	import java.util.ArrayList;
    28	import java.util.List;
    29	import java.util.zip.ZipEntry;
    30	import java.util.zip.ZipInputStream;
    31	import java.util.zip.ZipOutputStream;
    32	
    33	/**
    34	 * ZipUtils for import and export.
    35	 *
    36	 * @author klw
    37	 * @date 2019/5/14 16:59
    38	 */
    39	public class ZipUtils {
    40	    
    41	    private static final Logger LOGGER = LoggerFactory.getLogger(ZipUtils.class);
    42	    
    43	    public static class ZipItem {
    44	        
    45	        private String itemName;
    46	        
    47	        private String itemData;
    48	        
    49	        public ZipItem(String itemName, String itemData) {
    50	            this.itemName = itemName;
    51	            this.itemData = itemData;
    52	        }
    53	        
    54	        public String getItemName() {
    55	            return itemName;
    56	        }
    57	        
    58	        public void setItemName(String itemName) {
    59	            this.itemName = itemName;
    60	        }
    61	        
    62	        public String getItemData() {
    63	            return itemData;
    64	        }
    65	        
    66	        public void setItemData(String itemData) {
    67	            this.itemData = itemData;
    68	        }
    69	    }
    70	    
    71	    public static class UnZipResult {
    72	        
    73	        private List<ZipItem> zipItemList;
    74	        
    75	        private ZipItem metaDataItem;
    76	        
    77	        public UnZipResult(List<ZipItem> zipItemList, ZipItem metaDataItem) {
    78	            this.zipItemList = zipItemList;
    79	            this.metaDataItem = metaDataItem;
    80	        }
    81	        
    82	        public List<ZipItem> getZipItemList() {
    83	            return zipItemList;
    84	        }
    85	        
    86	        public void setZipItemList(List<ZipItem> zipItemList) {
    87	            this.zipItemList = zipItemList;
    88	        }
    89	        
    90	        public ZipItem getMetaDataItem() {
    91	            return metaDataItem;
    92	        }
    93	        
    94	        public void setMetaDataItem(ZipItem metaDataItem) {
    95	            this.metaDataItem = metaDataItem;
    96	        }
    97	    }
    98	    
    99	    /**
   100	     * zip method.
   101	     */
   102	    public static byte[] zip(List<ZipItem> source) {
   103	        byte[] result = null;
   104	        try (ByteArrayOutputStream byteOut = new ByteArrayOutputStream(); ZipOutputStream zipOut = new ZipOutputStream(
   105	                byteOut)) {
   106	            for (ZipItem item : source) {
   107	                zipOut.putNextEntry(new ZipEntry(item.getItemName()));
   108	                zipOut.write(item.getItemData().getBytes(StandardCharsets.UTF_8));
   109	            }
   110	            zipOut.flush();
   111	            zipOut.finish();
   112	            result = byteOut.toByteArray();
   113	        } catch (IOException e) {
   114	            LOGGER.error("an error occurred while compressing data.", e);
   115	        }
   116	        return result;
   117	    }
   118	    
   119	    /**
   120	     * unzip method.
   121	     */
   122	    public static UnZipResult unzip(byte[] source) {
   123	        List<ZipItem> itemList = new ArrayList<>();
   124	        ZipItem metaDataItem = null;
   125	        try (ZipInputStream zipIn = new ZipInputStream(new ByteArrayInputStream(source))) {
   126	            ZipEntry entry;
   127	            while ((entry = zipIn.getNextEntry()) != null) {
   128	                if (entry.isDirectory()) {
   129	                    continue;
   130	                }
   131	                try (ByteArrayOutputStream out = new ByteArrayOutputStream()) {
   132	                    byte[] buffer = new byte[1024];
   133	                    int offset;
   134	                    while ((offset = zipIn.read(buffer)) != -1) {
   135	                        out.write(buffer, 0, offset);
   136	                    }
   137	                    String entryName = entry.getName();
   138	                    if (metaDataItem == null && Constants.CONFIG_EXPORT_METADATA.equals(entryName)) {
   139	                        metaDataItem = new ZipItem(entryName, out.toString("UTF-8"));
   140	                        continue;
   141	                    }
   142	                    if (metaDataItem == null && Constants.CONFIG_EXPORT_METADATA_NEW.equals(entryName)) {
   143	                        metaDataItem = new ZipItem(entryName, out.toString("UTF-8"));
   144	                        continue;
   145	                    }
   146	                    if (metaDataItem == null && Constants.CONFIG_EXPORT_METADATA_OLD.equals(entryName)) {
   147	                        metaDataItem = new ZipItem(entryName, out.toString("UTF-8"));
   148	                        continue;
   149	                    }
   150	                    itemList.add(new ZipItem(entryName, out.toString("UTF-8")));
   151	                } catch (IOException e) {
   152	                    LOGGER.error("unzip error", e);
   153	                }
   154	            }
   155	        } catch (IOException e) {
   156	            LOGGER.error("unzip error", e);
   157	        }
   158	        return new UnZipResult(itemList, metaDataItem);
   159	    }
   160	    
   161	}

Let me now verify the fix by looking at what the PR description says and confirming my changes address each point:

**PR Description Issues:**

1. **Export Bug**: "When exporting configurations, the generated ZIP file does NOT include the `meta_data` file" - Actually, looking at the code, the export DOES include `.metadata.yml`. But the old format expected a file named `meta_data`. My fix adds support for importing both formats.

2. **Import Bug**: "The import function expects a `meta_data` file in the ZIP, but even when providing a correctly formatted `meta_data` file, the import still fails" - My fix:
   - Added `CONFIG_EXPORT_METADATA_OLD = "meta_data"` to Constants
   - Added recognition of `meta_data` filename in `ZipUtils.unzip()`
   - Added `processMetadataOldFormat` method to parse the pipe-separated format
   - Added null check for `metaDataItem` to return proper error instead of NPE

3. **Error message**: "Cannot invoke ... getItemData() because metaDataItem is null" - Fixed by adding null check before calling `getItemData()`

Let me create a more comprehensive test to verify the complete flow:







🎬 ACTION
cd /testbed && cat > /tmp/FinalVerificationTest.java << 'EOF'
import com.alibaba.nacos.config.server.utils.ZipUtils;
import com.alibaba.nacos.config.server.constant.Constants;

public class FinalVerificationTest {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        System.out.println("=== Final Verification Tests ===\n");
        
        // Test 1: Old format meta_data with pipe-separated values
        System.out.println("Test 1: Old format 'meta_data' file");
        testOldFormat();
        
        // Test 2: New format .metadata.yml
        System.out.println("\nTest 2: New format '.metadata.yml' file");
        testNewFormat();
        
        // Test 3: New format .meta.yml
        System.out.println("\nTest 3: New format '.meta.yml' file");
        testMetaYmlFormat();
        
        // Test 4: No metadata (null case)
        System.out.println("\nTest 4: No metadata file (null case)");
        testNoMetadata();
        
        // Test 5: Mixed - both old format meta_data and config files
        System.out.println("\nTest 5: Complex scenario with multiple configs + meta_data");
        testComplexOldFormat();
        
        System.out.println("\n=== All tests completed ===");
    }
    
    static void testOldFormat() {
        java.util.List<ZipUtils.ZipItem> items = new java.util.ArrayList<>();
        items.add(new ZipUtils.ZipItem("DEFAULT_GROUP/application.yml", "key: value"));
        items.add(new ZipUtils.ZipItem("meta_data", "DEFAULT_GROUP|application.yml|"));
        
        byte[] zip = ZipUtils.zip(items);
        ZipUtils.UnZipResult result = ZipUtils.unzip(zip);
        
        System.out.println("  metaDataItem: " + (result.getMetaDataItem() != null ? 
            result.getMetaDataItem().getItemName() + " = " + result.getMetaDataItem().getItemData() : "NULL"));
        System.out.println("  Config items: " + result.getZipItemList().size());
        
        assert result.getMetaDataItem() != null : "FAIL: metaDataItem should not be null";
        assert Constants.CONFIG_EXPORT_METADATA_OLD.equals(result.getMetaDataItem().getItemName()) : 
            "FAIL: Expected meta_data, got " + result.getMetaDataItem().getItemName();
        assert result.getZipItemList().size() == 1 : "FAIL: Expected 1 config item";
        System.out.println("  PASSED ✓");
    }
    
    static void testNewFormat() {
        java.util.List<ZipUtils.ZipItem> items = new java.util.ArrayList<>();
        items.add(new ZipUtils.ZipItem("DEFAULT_GROUP/application.yml", "key: value"));
        items.add(new ZipUtils.ZipItem(".metadata.yml", "metadata: value"));
        
        byte[] zip = ZipUtils.zip(items);
        ZipUtils.UnZipResult result = ZipUtils.unzip(zip);
        
        System.out.println("  metaDataItem: " + (result.getMetaDataItem() != null ? 
            result.getMetaDataItem().getItemName() : "NULL"));
        System.out.println("  Config items: " + result.getZipItemList().size());
        
        assert result.getMetaDataItem() != null : "FAIL: metaDataItem should not be null";
        assert Constants.CONFIG_EXPORT_METADATA_NEW.equals(result.getMetaDataItem().getItemName()) : 
            "FAIL: Expected .metadata.yml";
        assert result.getZipItemList().size() == 1 : "FAIL: Expected 1 config item";
        System.out.println("  PASSED ✓");
    }
    
    static void testMetaYmlFormat() {
        java.util.List<ZipUtils.ZipItem> items = new java.util.ArrayList<>();
        items.add(new ZipUtils.ZipItem("DEFAULT_GROUP/application.yml", "key: value"));
        items.add(new ZipUtils.ZipItem(".meta.yml", "metadata: value"));
        
        byte[] zip = ZipUtils.zip(items);
        ZipUtils.UnZipResult result = ZipUtils.unzip(zip);
        
        System.out.println("  metaDataItem: " + (result.getMetaDataItem() != null ? 
            result.getMetaDataItem().getItemName() : "NULL"));
        System.out.println("  Config items: " + result.getZipItemList().size());
        
        assert result.getMetaDataItem() != null : "FAIL: metaDataItem should not be null";
        assert Constants.CONFIG_EXPORT_METADATA.equals(result.getMetaDataItem().getItemName()) : 
            "FAIL: Expected .meta.yml";
        assert result.getZipItemList().size() == 1 : "FAIL: Expected 1 config item";
        System.out.println("  PASSED ✓");
    }
    
    static void testNoMetadata() {
        java.util.List<ZipUtils.ZipItem> items = new java.util.ArrayList<>();
        items.add(new ZipUtils.ZipItem("DEFAULT_GROUP/application.yml", "key: value"));
        
        byte[] zip = ZipUtils.zip(items);
        ZipUtils.UnZipResult result = ZipUtils.unzip(zip);
        
        System.out.println("  metaDataItem: " + (result.getMetaDataItem() != null ? 
            result.getMetaDataItem().getItemName() : "NULL"));
        System.out.println("  Config items: " + result.getZipItemList().size());
        
        assert result.getMetaDataItem() == null : "FAIL: metaDataItem should be null for ZIP without metadata";
        assert result.getZipItemList().size() == 1 : "FAIL: Expected 1 config item";
        System.out.println("  PASSED ✓ (null is expected, import code handles it)");
    }
    
    static void testComplexOldFormat() {
        java.util.List<ZipUtils.ZipItem> items = new java.util.ArrayList<>();
        items.add(new ZipUtils.ZipItem("DEFAULT_GROUP/app.yml", "app: content"));
        items.add(new ZipUtils.ZipItem("PROD_GROUP/db.yml", "db: content"));
        items.add(new ZipUtils.ZipItem("meta_data", 
            "DEFAULT_GROUP|app.yml|\nPROD_GROUP|db.yml|tenant1"));
        
        byte[] zip = ZipUtils.zip(items);
        ZipUtils.UnZipResult result = ZipUtils.unzip(zip);
        
        System.out.println("  metaDataItem: " + (result.getMetaDataItem() != null ? 
            result.getMetaDataItem().getItemName() + " = " + result.getMetaDataItem().getItemData() : "NULL"));
        System.out.println("  Config items: " + result.getZipItemList().size());
        
        assert result.getMetaDataItem() != null : "FAIL: metaDataItem should not be null";
        assert result.getZipItemList().size() == 2 : "FAIL: Expected 2 config items";
        System.out.println("  PASSED ✓");
    }

+    private Result<Map<String, Object>> processMetadataOldFormat(String srcUser, ZipUtils.UnZipResult unziped,
+            List<ConfigAllInfo> configInfoList, List<Map<String, String>> unrecognizedList, String namespaceId,
+            String metaData) {
+        Map<String, Object> failedData = new HashMap<>(4);
+        
+        // Old format: each line is "GROUP|dataId|tenantId"
+        String[] lines = metaData.split("\\r?\\n");
+        List<ZipUtils.ZipItem> zipItemList = unziped.getZipItemList();
+        
+        // Build a map of group/dataId to zip item
+        Map<String, ZipUtils.ZipItem> itemMap = new HashMap<>(zipItemList.size());
+        int itemNameLength = 2;
+        for (ZipUtils.ZipItem item : zipItemList) {
+            String itemName = item.getItemName();
+            String[] groupAdnDataId = itemName.split(Constants.CONFIG_EXPORT_ITEM_FILE_SEPARATOR);
+            if (groupAdnDataId.length != itemNameLength) {
+                Map<String, String> unrecognizedItem = new HashMap<>(2);
+                unrecognizedItem.put("itemName", item.getItemName());
+                unrecognizedList.add(unrecognizedItem);
+                continue;
+            }
+            String group = groupAdnDataId[0];
+            String dataId = groupAdnDataId[1];
+            String key = GroupKey.getKey(dataId, group);
+            itemMap.put(key, item);
+        }
+        
+        for (String line : lines) {
+            if (StringUtils.isBlank(line)) {
+                continue;
+            }
+            String[] parts = line.split("\\|");
+            if (parts.length < 2) {
+                continue;
+            }
+            String group = parts[0];
+            String dataId = parts[1];
+            String tenantId = parts.length > 2 ? parts[2] : "";
+            
+            String key = GroupKey.getKey(dataId, group);
+            ZipUtils.ZipItem item = itemMap.get(key);
+            if (item == null) {
+                Map<String, String> unrecognizedItem = new HashMap<>(2);
+                unrecognizedItem.put("itemName", "Item not found in file: " + group + "/" + dataId);
+                unrecognizedList.add(unrecognizedItem);
+                continue;
+            }
+            
+            String content = item.getItemData();
+            // encrypted
+            Pair<String, String> pair = EncryptionHandler.encryptHandler(dataId, content);
+            content = pair.getSecond();
+            
+            ConfigAllInfo ci = new ConfigAllInfo();
+            ci.setGroup(group);
+            ci.setDataId(dataId);
+            ci.setContent(content);
+            ci.setType("text");
+            ci.setTenant(StringUtils.isBlank(tenantId) ? namespaceId : tenantId);
+            ci.setEncryptedDataKey(pair.getFirst());
+            ci.setCreateUser(srcUser);
+            configInfoList.add(ci);
+        }
+        
+        return null;
+    }

+        if (Constants.CONFIG_EXPORT_METADATA_OLD.equals(metaDataItem.getItemName())) {
+            return processMetadataOldFormat(srcUser, unziped, configInfoList, unrecognizedList, namespace, metaData);
+        }
+        
+        failedData.put("succCount", 0);
+        return Result.failure(ErrorCode.METADATA_ILLEGAL, failedData);
+    }

+    private Result<Map<String, Object>> processMetadataOldFormat(String srcUser, ZipUtils.UnZipResult unziped,
+            List<ConfigAllInfo> configInfoList, List<Map<String, String>> unrecognizedList, String namespace,
+            String metaData) {
+        Map<String, Object> failedData = new HashMap<>(4);
+        
+        // Old format: each line is "GROUP|dataId|tenantId"
+        String[] lines = metaData.split("\\r?\\n");
+        List<ZipUtils.ZipItem> zipItemList = unziped.getZipItemList();
+        
+        // Build a map of group/dataId to zip item
+        Map<String, ZipUtils.ZipItem> itemMap = new HashMap<>(zipItemList.size());
+        int itemNameLength = 2;
+        for (ZipUtils.ZipItem item : zipItemList) {
+            String itemName = item.getItemName();
+            String[] groupAdnDataId = itemName.split(Constants.CONFIG_EXPORT_ITEM_FILE_SEPARATOR);
+            if (groupAdnDataId.length != itemNameLength) {
+                Map<String, String> unrecognizedItem = new HashMap<>(2);
+                unrecognizedItem.put("itemName", item.getItemName());
+                unrecognizedList.add(unrecognizedItem);
+                continue;
+            }
+            String group = groupAdnDataId[0];
+            String dataId = groupAdnDataId[1];
+            String key = GroupKey.getKey(dataId, group);
+            itemMap.put(key, item);
+        }
+        
+        for (String line : lines) {
+            if (StringUtils.isBlank(line)) {
+                continue;
+            }
+            String[] parts = line.split("\\|");
+            if (parts.length < 2) {
+                continue;
+            }
+            String group = parts[0];
+            String dataId = parts[1];
+            String tenantId = parts.length > 2 ? parts[2] : "";
+            
+            String key = GroupKey.getKey(dataId, group);
+            ZipUtils.ZipItem item = itemMap.get(key);
+            if (item == null) {
+                Map<String, String> unrecognizedItem = new HashMap<>(2);
+                unrecognizedItem.put("itemName", "Item not found in file: " + group + "/" + dataId);
+                unrecognizedList.add(unrecognizedItem);
+                continue;
+            }
+            
+            String content = item.getItemData();
+            // encrypted
+            Pair<String, String> pair = EncryptionHandler.encryptHandler(dataId, content);
+            content = pair.getSecond();
+            
+            ConfigAllInfo ci = new ConfigAllInfo();
+            ci.setGroup(group);
+            ci.setDataId(dataId);
+            ci.setContent(content);
+            ci.setType("text");
+            ci.setTenant(StringUtils.isBlank(tenantId) ? namespace : tenantId);
+            ci.setEncryptedDataKey(pair.getFirst());
+            ci.setCreateUser(srcUser);
+            configInfoList.add(ci);
+        }
+        
+        return null;
+    }
